Li Shizeng Reports on His Impressions of Traveling in Europe

| At the Central Memorial Weekly |

(Nanjing) The Central Government held the 74th Memorial Weekly service for the Premier at 8:00 AM on the 17th, attended by Huang Jichen, Wang Qi, Ye Chucang, Xie Zuomin, Dai Kuisheng, Zhang Weicun, Li Yuying, Chu Minyi, and staff members, totaling over six hundred people. It was chaired by Ye Chucang. Li Yuying reported, mainly stating that he spent the most time in Geneva during his trip to Europe. Various international organizations and institutions, whether political, economic, or academic, are very developed and are all gathered in Switzerland. Therefore, Geneva has almost become an international metropolis, proving that international cooperation and mutual assistance are suitable for modern needs. The Premier's legacy includes the idea that human evolution should be based on the principle of mutual assistance. The League of Nations was established based on the spirit of cooperation and mutual assistance. The methods and directions for resolving the Sino-Japanese problem were correct, although the decisive measure of economic sanctions could not be used. However, this is only a difference in degree, proving that the League of Nations is for the majority and cannot rely on a few countries to be arbitrary. He attended the World Cultural Cooperation Association on behalf of Mr. Zhihui. The association holds an annual meeting every July. This time, it was decided to establish an international library in Geneva to promote the World Cultural Cooperation Movement. Upon his return, he reported everything to Mr. Wu, who was very satisfied. Finally, he had some thoughts: all comrades should abide by the Premier's legacy that human evolution should be based on the principle of cooperation and mutual assistance, sincerely unite, and work together. Only then will the country have a way to be saved. On a larger and longer-term scale, we can solve world problems and achieve the Premier's ideal of a world of great harmony. After finishing his speech, the meeting was adjourned. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th)

Principles of the People's Self-Defense Corps Law

Glimpses of the Draft Content

(Nanjing) The draft principles of the People's Self-Defense Corps Law, drafted by the Ministry of Interior, the General Staff, the Ministry of Military Administration, and the Training and Supervision Department, has been submitted to the Political Council for discussion. Its contents are roughly as follows: the People's Self-Defense Corps is divided into three types: one is the standing team, which is composed of strong men of a certain age and is the backbone of the People's Self-Defense Corps, adopting a combined recruitment and conscription system; the second is the training team, which gathers and trains young people aged 18 to 19, with the aim of training young people first and gradually popularizing it to all strong men; the third is the strong men's team, the main purpose of which is to organize the people. In terms of organization, a three-level system of provinces, districts, and counties is adopted to establish a system. In terms of training, both political and military aspects are emphasized to enlighten the general members of the corps on the national and ethnic ideology. In terms of funding, the province will coordinate and distribute the funds to avoid the malpractice of local fundraising and extorting the people. In terms of conscription, the principles of obligation and balance will be followed to avoid resentment from the people. (Special dispatch on the 17th)

The Fourth Batch of Antiquities to be Transported South from Peiping Tomorrow

Japanese Government Convenes Local Governors Conference

Saito Delivers an Address, Expressing That He Will Not Step Down Temporarily

Uchida Delivers a Speech, Urging National Unity

The Japanese Political Situation Remains in Turmoil

(Tokyo) The Japanese cabinet convened a local governors conference at the Prime Minister's official residence at 9:00 AM this morning, lasting for one week. More than 40 governors from across the country attended. Finance Minister Takahashi first delivered a speech on the points to be noted in the implementation of the new budget and the Japanese government's fiscal and tax system reorganization policy. Justice Minister Oyama delivered a speech on strategies to deal with the Communist Party and various anti-imperialist organizations. Interior Minister Yamamoto delivered a speech on addressing internal turmoil and various domestic political issues. Prime Minister Saito said that since taking office last June, he recognized the independence of "Manchukuo" on September 15 and clashed with the League of Nations over the Manchurian issue, leading to the withdrawal from the League of Nations on March 27. The policy to be adopted in the future has been clearly indicated in the Emperor's edict. Everyone should abide by the edict and lead the local people. This year's budget increased by 400 million yuan compared to last year. There is currently no hope of increasing revenue, and it is not a time to increase taxes. Therefore, we will issue public bonds to overcome this severe period. Currently, there are slight signs of hope in the economic sector. I hope that everyone can step up the promotion of local people's self-reliance. Since I formed the cabinet, I have made great efforts to eliminate malpractices in the political arena, and the results are remarkable.

However, the extraordinary situation has not been resolved, and the cabinet's mission remains arduous. There are rumors about the future of the political situation. Everyone should respect themselves, not be misled, and redouble their efforts to save the country's future, etc. From this, it can be seen that Prime Minister Saito still expressed his reluctance to leave office. (China United Press dispatch on the 17th)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Uchida delivered a speech at the local governors conference today, saying that Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations seems to have put it in a difficult international position, but judging from the recent developments, there is no need to panic. To safely pass through the difficulties of the future, national unity is urgently needed, etc. (Reuters dispatch on the 17th)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito's instructions at the local governors conference today mentioned the future of the political situation, saying that the government is determined to move forward with the cooperation of the people. It is known that Prime Minister Saito will wait for Finance Minister Takahashi to resign after the May 15th Incident is resolved, and will decide to reorganize the cabinet and continue to maintain it. (Electric News Agency dispatch on the 17th)

(Tokyo) The future of the Japanese political situation is still unstable. Finance Minister Takahashi is prepared to submit his resignation to Prime Minister Saito after the local governors conference ends. Because the future of the political situation is still unstable, the agencies of various provinces have not started new projects for the new year. In the Seiyukai, those who actively urge Takahashi to step down are from the Suzuki faction. Others, such as the Tokonami and Kuhara factions, are temporarily supporting Takahashi to continue in office. The internal opinions of the only opposition party have not been unified. The future of the Japanese political situation remains in turmoil. (China United Press dispatch on the 17th)

Anti-Dumping Investigation Committee

The results have been reviewed in two meetings. Several foreign goods have been found to have dumping behavior and tariffs will soon be implemented to protect domestic goods. To clarify the cost of these foreign goods and their selling prices in the domestic market, calculations are being made to determine the cost of shipping to China, plus freight and customs duties, and the fair market price for sale in China. If the selling price exceeds the fair price, the goods will be considered dumped. A request has been sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, instructing our country's consulates abroad to investigate and report back. (17th Dispatch)

Roosevelt Will Send Message to Congress

Requesting to Negotiate Tax Treaty Privileges

French President Sends Letter Wishing Herriot a Safe Journey

US Domestic Relief Needs Funds, Plans to Issue Bonds

▲National News Agency, Washington, 16th – It was learned today that President Roosevelt has drafted four special messages to Congress, which will be sent to the Senate and House of Representatives in the next few days. It is said that the first message requests the power to negotiate mutual tariff agreements after discussions with delegations from various countries coming here for economic events and formal meetings. The second message concerns the issuance of bonds, which is necessary to relieve the current situation of farmer mortgages and implement procedures for placing the unemployed. It is expected that the President will request the issuance of at least 30 billion US dollars in bonds this year. Emergency legislation is progressing well. The President now believes that permanent solutions to banking problems and railway affairs can be pursued. The other two messages relate to these two issues.

▲Havas, Le Havre, France, 17th – Former Prime Minister Herriot, on board the "Île de France" for the US to attend the Washington economic talks, received a letter from the President upon boarding the ship, stating, "As you set sail, I write these few lines to express my best wishes and wish you a pleasant journey, a successful mission, and a safe return."

Chairman of the US Immigration Committee Advocates

Revising Immigration Laws

To Crack Down on Chinese Entering from Mexico

▲National News Agency, Washington, 16th – Mr. Diekstein, Chairman of the Immigration Committee of the US House of Representatives, has recently completed his plan to revise US immigration laws, nationality laws, and repatriation procedures, for adoption by this session of Congress. The main points include: (1) Preventing foreign nationals from entering the country from Cuba, Mexico, and other places; (2) Improving repatriation administration; (3) Revising nationality laws for the sake of uniformity and clarity; (4) Re-examining all proposals concerning immigration numbers carefully for the sake of uniformity; (5) Humanitarian improvements to immigration law, such as allowing elderly parents of American citizens to enter the country, etc. Mr. Diekstein said that various nationality laws already in place really need to be thoroughly re-evaluated. The reason is that in recent years, Congress has only known how to pass various amendments, making unlimited additions and deletions to the original nationality laws, and no new nationality law has emerged to replace them, resulting in the current chaotic state of American nationality, making it impossible for non-experts in nationality law to understand the general situation. Therefore, it should be reorganized today to make it simple and easy to understand. As for the number of immigrants entering the country, it must be calculated together with European countries in the future to be accurate, he said. Mr. Diekstein is quite concerned about the cruelty of repatriation treatment and plans to request members of the House to form a special committee to review the matter. As for foreign nationals mixing into the US from Cuba and the coastal areas are the most prevalent. A large number of Japanese and Chinese are also entering illegally on the Mexican border. They use many methods, so to prevent this illegal act, it is necessary to first investigate the methods they commonly use, and then establish regulations to strictly prohibit them. At the same time, it is also possible to consider whether the repatriation procedures are inhumane so that these habitual offenders cannot re-enter illegally, he said.

Retrial of the British Engineers Case

Russian Prosecutor Involves Court Issues

Criticizes the Remarks of British Parliamentarians

Defendant's Bribery is True, Cannot Be Pardoned According to Law

After Final Arguments, Verdict Expected Today or Tomorrow

▲Reuters, Moscow, 16th – The Soviet Russian prosecutor gave his summary of the case against the six Britons tonight during the retrial of the Vickers engineers' case. He offered much criticism of Britain. The retrial resumed at 9:15 PM tonight, and the audience seats in the courtroom were full. The head of the expert committee first answered questions raised by lawyer Munch-Hurse today, saying that a piece of metal could pass through the protective net of the turbine and damage the turbine. The turbines supplied by Vickers had been tested and were indeed different from what was guaranteed, and the technicians were also negligent in correcting the defects of the turbine blades. The expert committee found a turbine in the Moscow power plant that was not supplied by Vickers. Munch-Hurse immediately retorted, saying that he could not accept this answer satisfactorily. If the guarantee conditions had not been fulfilled, then why did the Soviet Union not notify the company concerned? Deputy Prosecutor Roginsky warned the defendant that he was not trying Vickers but was trying its employees. Munch-Hurse replied that the expert committee's answer was directed at Vickers, not at the defendant. Prosecutor Vyshinsky summarized the proceedings of the past four days, read out his lengthy written remarks, and said that our enemies are trying to suppress us in every way. I hope that the outcome of this case can strike a blow against our enemies. We do not want to allow others to interfere in our internal affairs. Capitalists do not like Soviet courts because they are class courts. British Member of Parliament Patrick said that he was ashamed to see Soviet judges smoking while hearing cases and that he himself had sat on hard wooden chairs. According to the British, the difference between Soviet and British courts is that British courts advocate fairness, while the Soviet Union is the opposite. (Patrick is a British Conservative MP who stated in the House of Commons on April 5 that he had observed a trial in Moscow and felt that the Soviet court was an instrument of class warfare.) At this point, the prosecutor cited Marx's saying that British courts have two kinds of laws, one for the rich and one for the poor. He also said that the British also use torture in India, and there are recent examples to prove it. The only place in the world with true fairness is Russia. Munch-Hurse and Thornton followed the instructions of the British White Paper and tried to insult the Soviet court, but no matter what, they could not prove that they had been mistreated by the Soviet Union. Munch-Hurse initially gave false testimony during the political investigation period and then asked for forgiveness for his lies. Regarding this point, I hope that the court will not pay attention to the petitions issued by the defendants Munch-Hurse Kerschney and Thornton regarding how the Soviet Union treated them. The Russians Vareni and Kutuzova are in league with the most heinous enemies, which is very wrong. The Russian defendants are slackers. Although the act of slacking has now been stopped, the defendants must not be pardoned. The prosecutor pointed out that the crimes of Munch-Hurse and Thornton were the most disgusting and that these two were more dangerous than the Russian defendants. The prosecutor then explained the definition of the term "espionage" to the court using the British Standard Dictionary, saying that the Soviet Union's definition of this term is the same as that of the United Kingdom. He also said that anyone who seeks news about people's political feelings is not committing espionage. The prosecutor later spoke about bribery, saying that Munch-Hurse had failed to explain whether the 3,000 rubles he gave to Polgov were a gift or a loan. British engineers might think that giving a small amount of money is not bribery in the Soviet Union. Know that this matter is bribery even under British law. Munch-Hurse and Thornton both knew that they would be severely punished because from the Soviet standpoint, bribery is a major crime. The court adjourned at 11:25 PM and will resume at 11:00 AM tomorrow morning. The defendants' lawyers will speak in defense at that time, and then the defendants will make their final statements. It is expected that the verdict can be rendered on Tuesday or Wednesday morning.

Defendant Raises Ten Questions

During the secret trial this morning, defendant Munch-Hurse raised ten questions to the technical advisory committee of the court, requesting answers. The court immediately decided that eight of the questions could be answered by the committee. The two items that were crossed out were those concerning the responsibility of Vickers Company. The court held that the persons being tried in this case were not the company or its representatives, but individual citizens, who were accused of criminal acts. Therefore, the court cannot accept these two questions. After this decision, the court announced that it would reopen at 7:00 PM to publish the Technical Committee's answers to Munch's questions. (Tass News Agency, 16th)

Russian Newspaper Publishes Diplomatic Talks Regarding Britain

The talks between Soviet People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov and British Ambassador Lord Voffan regarding the engineer case have been published. The Soviet government organ Izvestia commented that "the British people do not know the content of the talks, so they cannot know the calmness and firm attitude expressed by Foreign Commissar Litvinov to Lord Voffan. This is quite regrettable. Litvinov made it clear to Voffan that although the Soviet government was under various threats, it was unwilling to give up its right to review all the documents in the case and submit them to the court. The court hearing has proved that it would have been better if the British government had shown calmness similar to that of Soviet Russia." The communist organ Pravda stated, "The British ambassador not only demanded that Litvinov immediately release the defendants and declare them innocent, but also wanted the Soviet government to guarantee that such accidents would not happen again in the future. His attitude can be described as strange." (Havas News Agency, 16th)

Six British Defendants May Not Escape Death in Soviet Russia

Russian Prosecutor Vyshinsky did not state what penalties should be imposed if the charges of sabotage and espionage against the six Britons were true, but judging from the current situation, the Britons may not escape death. Vyshinsky said in his closing remarks today that all defendants except Grigore should be sentenced to death. However, the Soviet court does not act out of revenge or cruelty, but if the court believes that it is necessary to implement the strictest measures against the criminals, then do not hesitate. (National News Agency, Moscow, 15th)

British Independent Labour Party Sympathizes with Russia British

The British Independent Labour Party's annual conference passed a resolution stating that the party fully sympathizes with Soviet Russia. If the British-Russian conflict escalates into open hostility, it will declare a general strike to respond. Party leader Brockway declared that "Our party's open support for Soviet Russia and opposition to the British government under the current circumstances should be known to the world. We know that this attitude is not unique to our party, and we must strive to unite workers all over the world and resist the threat of war by all means and take the opportunity to overthrow the government and the capitalism it represents." The conference also unanimously passed a resolution opposing the police's tyrannical actions against unemployed workers. (Havas News Agency, London, 17th)

Yesterday's Continued Trial Proceedings

The Wikers Company Technicians Case Continued This Morning, Prosecutor Vyshinsky Presented the Case, As Sharp As Before, While Several English Defendants Gradually Showed Signs of Excessive Agitation and Mental Exhaustion. The Prosecutor Spoke in Detail About the Shortcomings of the Wikers Machines, Hoping to Prove That the Damage to the Machines They Sent Was Purely Due to Sabotage. The Prosecutor Also Praised MacDonald's Courage in Admitting His Guilt, Saying That If These People Could Speak Honestly, Then MacDonald Could Be Said to Be Honest, and Also Brave, Much Braver Than the Soldier Thornton Who Served in the Mesopotamian Theater. The Prosecutor Also Pointed Out That the South African Technician Krushny Deliberately Ignored the Poor Performance of the Second Turbine, Saying That This Showed Krushny's Lack of Attention to Whether the Motor's Work Was Good or Bad. These Saboteurs Had Their Five-Year Plan in the Main Plant Supplying Electricity to the Moscow Area, and the Sabotage Began in 1928, Which Is Now the Fifth Year. Among the Defendants, There Is One Whose Crimes I Have Not Yet Been Able to Determine, and I Will Speak About It Again When I Bring Charges in the Future, He Said. This Statement Refers to Wikers Company Technician Gregory, Who Is Also Accused of Being a Saboteur and Engaging in Economic, Military, and Civil Espionage. The Prosecutor Also Said That the Crimes of the Other Defendants Are True, and I Have Photographs to Prove It. MacDonald Is an Experienced Detective, More Agile Than Others. He Was Discovered While Implementing Sabotage. The Information He Collected Has No Beneficial Relationship With the Wikers Company, He Said. The Prosecutor Referred to Thornton's Testimony in Court as Childish and Said That He Would Request the Most Severe Punishment to Be Imposed on the Russian Gusev, Who Admitted to Being a Saboteur and Spy. The Prosecutor Seems to Want to Ask the Judge to Sentence Gusev to Death. The Prosecutor Said That He Had a Lot of Evidence Against the English Technician Nordwall, and That There Were Four Points in Nordwall's Testimony Regarding the Gift of a Leather Jacket to Lobanov That Did Not Conform to the Facts. The Prosecutor Distinguished Between the Seriousness of the Crimes of the Russian Defendants, Saying That Shepetov's Crime Could Be Mitigated Because of His Confession, and He Did Not Want to Impose a Severe Punishment. As for Sokolukin, Who Worked With Thornton, He Was the One Who Sabotaged the Moscow No. 1 Power Plant and Should Be Severely Punished (Reuters Moscow, 17th).

Dutch-Japanese Arbitration Treaty

May Be Signed Today

▲Reuters Tokyo, 17th: The Cabinet Will Approve the Dutch-Japanese Arbitration Tomorrow, and Jiang Will Order the Japanese Ambassador to The Hague to Sign the Treaty.

▲Denstu Tokyo, 17th: The Main Points of the Dutch-Japanese Treaty Are As Follows: (1) All Disputes Between the Two Countries Will Be Resolved by the Permanent Mediation Committee in Principle. (2) The Two Countries Are Not Bound by the Decisions of the Committee. (3) The Composition of the Mediation Committee: Each Country Will Appoint One Member From Japan and the Netherlands, and Three Foreigners of Different Nationalities Will Be Selected and Added With the Agreement of Both Countries, for a Total of Five Members. (4) In Disputes Between Japan and the Netherlands, Matters Concerning the Interpretation of Laws and Treaties Will, With the Agreement of Both Countries, Be Submitted to Arbitration in The Hague or to the Arbitration Committee Established With the Agreement of Both Countries.

Aimed at Promoting National Ideology

▲Reuters Kobe, 17th: An Asian Youth Association Has Been Formed in Kobe, With Suzuki as Its President. At the Beginning of Its Establishment, It Announced the Following Aims: (1) To Strive to Promote Our Racial Ideology in Accordance With the Spirit of National Founding. (2) To Seek to Free the Asian People From the Yoke of the White Race. (3) To Overthrow Capitalism and Destroy International Weapons and Long-Standing Political Parties That Are Only Beneficial to the White Race.

No Investigation Has Been Conducted by People's Organizations in Hunan Province. Please Correct This in the Original Location. Regards, Chang Kai.

"Puppet State" and the Chinese Eastern Railway

Russo-Puppet Negotiations Have No Results

Guerrillas Active, Train Derailment

The Zi Lin Bao Harbin Dispatch of March 31st States That Railway Issues Are Currently Widely Discussed Among the People of Harbin, and Various Newspapers Are Also Reporting on This Matter in Lengthy Articles. The Final Outcome Cannot Be Predicted, So People Are Extremely Nervous. According to Reports Today, Last Week Railway Police Discovered Four Locomotives That Were Planning to Enter Russian Territory.

They Quickly Took Measures to Make Them Fall Into a Sidetrack to Avoid Driving Out of Manchuria. The Chinese Eastern Railway Ordered the Railway Police to Arrest Employees Who Interfered With the Locomotive's Actions. One of the Locomotives Was Blocked in Manzhouli, and the Five Russian Employees in the Car Were All Arrested and Escorted to Harbin. The "Manchukuo" Government Now Insists That It Is Illegal for Cars Traveling From West to East to Pass Through the Chinese Eastern Railway Route and Will Strictly Prohibit It. As for the Arrangement for the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Ussuri Railway to Exchange Trains in the East, the "Manchukuo" Authorities Do Not Want to Interfere, but Each Time the Ussuri Railway Should Hand Over Equally Good Cars to the Chinese Eastern Railway. The Requirements Put Forward by the Manzhouli Authorities Have Not Yet Been Answered by Kusnietsov, the Deputy Director of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and Instead, He Has Lodged a Serious Protest Due to the Recent Banditry in the Eastern Section, With One Passenger Train and One Freight Train Derailing One After Another. This Morning, Harbin Received News That a Passenger Train From Vladivostok to Harbin Derailded Near Hailin, Killing and Injuring Many Passengers. At the Same Time, Japanese Newspapers Also Claimed That Thousands of Bandits Were Gathered Near Five Stations, So Train Travel Is Very Dangerous.

The Issue of Soviet Goods Passing Through Manchuria From West to East and the Issue of Soviet Locomotives and Freight Cars Shipped From the Chinese Eastern Railway Last Year That Have Not Yet Been Returned Have Now Gradually Become Intense. The "Manchukuo" Director General of the Chinese Eastern Railway Has Repeatedly Lodged Protests With the Soviet Deputy Director General, But Has Not Received a Single Response. Therefore, Morita, the Japanese Vice Minister of Communications of "Manchukuo," Has Led Two Japanese Members to Harbin to Discuss the Issue With the Soviets. "Manchukuo" Representatives Have Met With the Russian Board of Directors Several Times, But With No Results. The Soviet Deputy Director General Only Said That He Had Reported the Matter to the Moscow Government. According to Soviet Practices, Goods Are Transported From Manzhouli Through the Chinese Eastern Railway to the Maritime Provinces. Soviet Manufactured Products Are All Government Monopolies, So These Goods Are Actually Owned by the Government. The Freight Is Generally Not Paid in Cash, but Only Entered Into the Company's Account as a Debt Owed by the Soviet Government, Which Has Reached 2 Million Gold Rubles Today. There Is Also an Account Book in the Company for Transactions With the Chinese Government. The Chinese Government Generally Does Not Pay Freight for Transporting Goods and Troops, but Instead Leaves the Debt in the Account. The Soviet Government Believes That the Soviet Union Has the Inherent Right to Do As the Chinese Government Does, So That the Debts on Both Sides Can Be Offset When They Are Equal in the Future. However, the "Manchukuo" Authorities Claim That There Are No Such Regulations for Transporting Goods in the Contract Between the Two Sides, So They Intend to Prohibit It. As for the Freight Cars That the Soviet Government Shipped Into Russian Territory Last Year, It Is Said That the Chinese Eastern Railway Did Not Pay for These Freight Cars. During the European War, the Allied Powers Purchased Many Goods in the United States and Transported Them to Vladivostok, and Then Shipped Them to Russia in Europe Via Manchuria. Among Them Was a Large Batch of Freight Cars Purchased by the British Government and Handed Over to the Russian Government, Which Were Disassembled and Transported to Harbin for Delivery, So That They Could Be Assembled in the Chinese Eastern Railway Factory. People Still Living in Harbin Can Prove This. Later, Due to the Russian Revolution, They Were Never Handed Over to the Russian Government, So the Soviet Government Should Now Inherit Them. The "Manchukuo" Authorities Claim That All of the Freight Cars of the Chinese Eastern Railway Are the Property of the Company. Yesterday, When Representatives of the "Manchukuo" Ministry of Communications Met With Soviet Deputy Director General Kusnietsov, Kusnietsov Said That All Freight Cars Belonging to the Chinese Eastern Railway Should Be Returned, But Those That the Soviet Government Believed Did Not Belong to the Chinese Eastern Railway Are Not Included. According to Russian Newspaper Reports, This Issue Is Now Extremely Difficult, But It Will Not Cause the Terrible Situation of Triggering a War, as Some Newspapers Have Said. Although There Have Been Rumors of a Mutiny in Siberia Recently, the Soviet Government Is Still Making Full Military Preparations for the Manchurian Issue to Prevent a Break. In Addition, Most of the Japanese Troops in Northern Manchuria Have Been Transferred to Jehol for Combat, and the Remaining Forces Are Very Weak. Starting a War at This Time Is the Most Foolish Thing to Do. Therefore, It Is Expected That Both Sides Can Eventually Negotiate a Satisfactory Solution.

Another Train Derailment Occurred on the Eastern Section of the Chinese Eastern Railway This Morning. This Proves That the Former Volunteer Army in That Area Has Now Reassembled and Is Trying to Hinder Railway Transportation and Harm Japanese Troops in Various Ways. After the Train Derailded, the Volunteer Army Immediately Opened Fire, Bombarding the Japanese Guards, Killing Three and Seriously Wounding Five. However, None of the Passengers Were Injured. The Driver Also Died Instantly Due to the Overturn of the Car. Soon After, the Following Train Arrived and Was Also Fiercely Bombarded. The Volunteer Army Obviously Thought That There Must Be Many Japanese People on Board. According to Railway Bureau Officials, Almost All of the Passenger Cars Were Destroyed in This Accident, and the Locomotive Also Needs Major Repairs. The Track Has Been Severely Damaged and Also Needs Three Days of Repairs. For the Sake of Caution, the Railway Bureau Has Now Suspended Night Passenger Trains.

Cai Tingkai Visits Guangdong Again

Cai Talks About His Willingness to Be in the Vanguard of the Anti-Japanese War

And Urges Chen Jitang to Take Full Responsibility for Suppressing the Communists

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the 19th Route Army Entered Guangdong From Fujian's Dongjiang, They Took the Road Through Meixian, Xingning, and Longchuan, and Turned Into Wengyuan in Beijiang, Gathering in a Certain Place in Beijiang to Await Orders to Go North. Cai Tingkai, Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army, Also Came to Guangdong From Fujian to Negotiate Departure Matters With the Guangdong Authorities. He Arrived in Hong Kong From Fujian by Ship on the 9th, Stayed in Hong Kong for One Day, and Negotiated With Politicians Living in Hong Kong. On the Afternoon of the 11th, He Took the Guangzhou-Kowloon Express to the Province Again. Dozens of Military and Political Figures Went to the Station to Welcome Him. After Cai Got Off the Train, He Accompanied Xiang Hanping, Commander of the Second Army, and Tan Qixiu, Commander of the 19th Brigade, to the Headquarters of the First Group Army to Visit Chen Jitang and Discuss the Great Plan of Resisting Japan and Suppressing the Communists. Chen Had Already Been Waiting at the Headquarters. Central Committee Members From the Southwest and Generals From the First Group Army Were All Present. They Had a Very Pleasant Conversation. Chen Also Held a Banquet at Headquarters to Welcome Cai. They Briefly Discussed the Current Situation During the Banquet and Dispersed With Great Enjoyment. According to Cai, Recent External Aggression and Internal Troubles Are Approaching. Both Japan and the Communists Are Enough to Destroy Us. There Is No Distinction Between Light and Heavy. We Should Deal With Them at the Same Time. Resisting Japan Is the Natural Duty of Soldiers. This Time Guangdong and Fujian Sent Troops. It Is Rumored That I Am Serving as the Commander-in-Chief, But I Think It Is Not Necessary to Pay Attention to the Name. I Am Only Determined to Resist Japan. Moreover, Fighting With Japan Is My Long-Cherished Wish. No Matter What the Name Is, I Am Happy to Take Responsibility and Be in the Vanguard for the Party and the Country. The Issue of Suppressing the Communists Is Also an Urgent Matter at Present. Chairman Chiang Recently Entered Jiangxi to Command the Suppression of the Communists and Telegraphically Instructed Me to Return to Guangdong and Urge Commander-in-Chief Bonan (Chen Jitang) to Take Full Responsibility for Suppressing the Communists in Jiangxi Province. The Central Government Will Give Him the Title of Commander-in-Chief or Commander-in-Chief of the Suppression of the Communists to Take Full Responsibility for the Suppression of the Communists in Jiangxi Province. However, When Talking About It Hasty, Bonan Did Not Make Any Formal Statement. It Is Probably Still Under Consideration Before He Can Agree. Recently, Some People Said That I Would Return to Guangdong to Attend the National Defense Committee and Negotiate the Resistance Against Japan. I Hope the Name Is Self-Explanatory. The National Defense Committee Is an Agency for Planning National Defense, Which Is Completely Different From Military Actions. The Measures of the Committee Depend on the Economy. Now That Most of the Items Have Been Decided, There Is No Need for the National Defense Committee to Hold a Meeting, and So On. On the 12th, the Southwest Political Affairs Council Held an Emergency Meeting and Invited Cai to Attend. Li Zongren Also Attended From the Sanatorium, Supported by Illness. They Discussed the Two Major Plans of Resisting Japan and Suppressing the Communists. The Meeting Lasted From 11:00 AM to 1:00 PM. The Security Was Extremely Tight, and the Details Are Not Known. (April 13th)

Chen Duxiu Submits a Document to the High Court

Claims No Attempt to Usurp the Republic of China

Suzhou Correspondence: Chen Duxiu and Others Are Currently Being Tried by Members of the High Court in Nanjing. Recently, Chen Personally Wrote a Statement and Submitted It to the High Court. The Statement Is Thousands of Words Long. The Content First States That His Revolution Over the Past 30 Years Has Been to Improve China. Second, the Purpose of Organizing the Communist Party Is to Resist Imperialism to Complete China's Independence, Resist Warlords and Bureaucrats to Realize National Unification, Improve the Lives of Farmers and Workers, and Realize the Thoroughly Democratic National Legislative Conference. He Also Declares That the Trotskyites Have Nothing to Do With the Jiangxi and Other Historical Factions. The Communist Party Exists in Various European and American Countries and Cannot Be Immediately Regarded as a Criminal. I (Chen Refers to Himself) Have No Intention to Usurp the Republic of China for the Party and the Country Now and in the Future. All Purposes and Actions Are to Support the Republic of China and Cannot Be Regarded as Harming the Republic of China. Otherwise, What Should Be Interpreted as the So-Called Republic of China? Finally, He Says That If the Court Does Not Completely Obey Special Forces, If It Still Thinks of Maintaining Some Judicial Independence Internally and Externally, It Should Unhesitatingly Declare Him Not Guilty and Order the Government to Pay Compensation for His Economic and Health Losses During His Detention. (April 17th)

The 21st Army

Organizes a Southwest Construction Committee Branch

Liu Xiang Concurrently Serves as Chairman

Tang Shizun and Others Serve as Standing Committee Members

Chongqing Correspondence: The 21st Army Headquarters Believes That Construction Projects Are Extremely Complex. In Addition to the Local Construction Projects in Various Counties, Which Have Been Ordered to Be Carried Out in Order by the County Magistrates and Township Chiefs in Accordance With the Department's Stipulated Guidelines, Large-Scale Construction Projects Concerning Non-Private Enterprises, Such as Water Conservancy, Electricity, and Road Administration, Are Related to Other Parties, Require People and Funds, and Are Extremely Complex. It Is Difficult to Achieve Results Without Setting Up Another Agency, Concentrating Talents, and Pooling Efforts. Therefore, in Accordance With Article 7 of the Organizational Law of the Construction Committee of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, a Southwest Construction Committee Branch Was Established in Chongqing. Liu Xiang, Superintendent of Sichuan Rehabilitation, Appointed Tang Shizun, Pan Wenhua, Wang Lingji, Wang Zuixu,

Liu Hangchen, Tang Hua, Gan Jiyong, Bo Youzhou, and Yuan Bin as Standing Committee Members. In Addition, Guo Changming, Zhang Zai, Yang Canzan, Lu Zuofu, He Beiheng, Chen Xuechi, Kang Xinru, Zhang Yujiu, Ren Wangnan, Wen Shaohe, Li Kuian, Zhou Yangchi, Hu Wenlan, Pan Changyou, Zhao Zisheng, Wang Yun Song, Li Xinwu, Ji Shuping, Wu Shuqi, Zhang Biguo, and Gao Xianjin Were Appointed as Committee Members to Cooperate. The Organizational Outline of the Southwest Construction Committee Branch Is Extracted Below:

Article 1: This Branch Is Organized in Accordance With Article 7 of the Organizational Law of the Construction Committee of the Executive Yuan of the National Government for the Sake of Developing Southwest Construction. Article 2: The Powers of This Branch Are As Follows: (1) This Branch Shall Follow Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Outline of National Construction and the Three Principles of the People to Design and Supervise Large-Scale Construction Projects Concerning Non-Private Enterprises. (2) Water Conservancy, Electricity, and Other State-Owned Enterprises That Do Not Belong to Various Departments and Responsible Agencies Shall Be Handled by This Branch at Its Discretion. (3) State-Owned Enterprises Belonging to Various Departments,

If the Relevant Agencies Have Not Been Held in the Southwest, the Branch May Also Handle Them at Its Discretion. (4) This Branch Shall Design, Implement, Supervise, and Evaluate the Projects It Handles in Order. Article 3: The Projects of This Branch Shall Be Divided Into the Following Categories According to the Needs of the Times and the Scope of the Region: (1) Those Within the Scope of Eastern and Southern Sichuan Shall Be Handled in Consultation With the Highest Military and Political Leaders in the Local Area. (2) Those Concerning the Entire Province of Sichuan Shall Be Handled in Consultation With All Parties Concerned. (3) Those Concerning Various Provinces in the Southwest Shall Be Handled in Consultation With the Governments of Various Provinces. Article 4: The Personnel of This Branch Are As Follows: (1) One Chairman Shall Be Appointed to Manage the Affairs of the Entire Branch, Concurrently Serving as the Superintendent of Sichuan Rehabilitation. (2) One Secretary-General Shall Be Appointed to Assist in the Affairs of the Branch. (3) Four Groups Shall Be Established: Industry, Commerce, Mining, and Transportation. Each Group Shall Have One Director and One Deputy Director, Who Shall Be Responsible for the Affairs of Each Group. All of Them Shall Be Appointed by the Superintendent of Sichuan Rehabilitation. (4) Seven Standing Committee Members and a Number of Committee Members Shall Be Appointed or Employed by the Superintendent of Sichuan Rehabilitation. Article 5: When Necessary, This Branch May Employ Domestic and Foreign Experts as Special Committee Members or Consultants. Article 6: This Branch Shall Be Located in Chongqing City. Article 7: This Branch Shall Hold a Standing Meeting at Least Once a Week and a General Meeting Once or Twice a Year, Which Shall Be Convened by the Chairman. Article 8: This Branch Needs a Lot of Funds to Prepare Various Projects. In Addition to Raising Funds Locally, We Welcome Overseas Chinese Investment and May Borrow Foreign Debt When Necessary to Develop the Projects. Article 9: The Meeting Rules and Detailed Rules of This Branch Shall Be Formulated Separately. Article 10: This Outline Shall Be Implemented From the Date of Promulgation. (Daily News Agency)

Songjiang

Zhang Wuxia Declares Innocent

When Fan Guozhong, the First Team Leader of the First District of the Waterborne Provincial Security Corps, Captured the Bandits Lin Yunquan and Zhong Shaoyun in a Restaurant Outside the East Gate of Songcheng, Zhang Wuxia, the Patrol Chief of the County Water Patrol Team, Was Also in the Restaurant and Was Escorted to the Court on Suspicion. Soon After, Lu Ada Was Captured and Tried Together. After the Prosecutor Filed a Public Prosecution Under the Law on Punishing Bandits, Zhang Yihuang, the Judge of the Criminal Court, Questioned Zhang Wuxia. Zhang Wuxia Hired Lawyer Zhang Baopei to Defend Him. At the End of the Trial, Zhang Wuxia Was Declared Not Guilty Today. Lin Yunquan, Zhong Shaoyun, and Lu Ada Were Each Sentenced to 14 Years in Prison. Zhang Wuxia Was Allowed to Be Released on Bail.

Capture of Kidnapping Bandits From Shaoxing

The Wuxian Public Security Bureau Received a Letter From the Shaoxing County Government in Zhejiang Province Stating That Criminals Wanted in Connection With Kidnapping Cases in the County Were Hiding Outside Xumen and Requested That They Be Investigated and Arrested. Taicang

Announcement of New Officials of the County Government

Since County Magistrate Hong Took Office, Zhao Qi Was Appointed as Secretary, Wang Yun as Director of the First Section, and Yu Shaoyao as Director of the Second Section. Most of the Other Section Members and Clerks Have Been Transferred.

Jin Yutong Rice Shop Goes Bankrupt

This Year, Silver Is Extremely Tight. Since the Beginning of Spring, More Than 40 Shops in the County Have Gone Bankrupt. Jin Yutong Rice Shop, Located East of Feiyun Bridge in the City, Has Been Open for More Than Ten Years. Recently, Due to a Lack of Turnover, It Announced Liquidation Yesterday and Was in Debt for More Than 30,000 Yuan.

Wuxi

Textile Mills Implement Work Reduction

The Shanghai Chinese Textile Mills Association Believes That the Price of Yarn Has Fallen Sharply, Stockpiles Have Accumulated, and Sales Have Been Stagnant, Which Has Had a Great Impact on the Future of the Textile Industry. Therefore, in Order to Reduce Production and Reverse the Decline, Work Reduction Measures Were Formulated, and Members Were Sent From the Shanghai Mills Association to Various Places to Urge and Assist in the Implementation. The Work Reduction Measures Stipulate That Work Will Be Suspended for Eight Days Each Month (Originally Four Days), and Daily Working Hours Will Also Be Shortened. However, This County Is a Developed Area for Industry and Commerce. There Are a Total of Seven Textile Mills, With More Than 30,000 Male and Female Workers. If Work Is Reduced Once, It May Be Related to the Livelihood of the Workers. Moreover, Most of the Textile Mills in This County Also Operate Weaving, and Most of the Cotton Yarn Produced Is Woven Into Cloth. Therefore, the Impact of the Sharp Drop in Yarn Prices Is Still Small. Therefore, Each Factory Has Been Hesitant to Implement It. Recently, Qingfeng Textile Mill in Zhou Shanbang Has Been the First to Implement Work Reduction Since the Previous Day, and Zhenxin Textile Mill in Taibaodun Will Also Implement Work Reduction This Week. However, Shenxin No. 3 Mill and Changxin Dyeing and Weaving Mill Have Not Yet Decided.

City News

Representative to the Washington Conference, Song Ziwen, Leaves for the United States This Afternoon

Liu Chongjie Carries Important Documents to Song for Reference

Wang and Song's Final Meeting This Morning to Discuss Everything

Whether Song Will Go to Europe Will Be Decided After Arriving in the United States

Song Ziwen, Our Country's Representative to the Washington World Economic Conference, Was Originally Scheduled to Leave Shanghai This Morning on the President Jackson Ship. It Has Been Changed to 12:00 This Afternoon, When the Ship Will Be Anchored and Leave Shanghai. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Believes That Song's Trip to the United States Is Important to Foreign Relations, So Liu Chongjie, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Personally Carried a Large Amount of External Documents From Nanjing to Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Handed Them to Song for Reference. Song Visited Wang Jingwei Again Yesterday Morning to Make the Final Consultation. At 5:00 PM, He Attended a Farewell Tea Party Held by Various Countries. Song Is Scheduled to Take a Customs Small Wheel From the New Customs Wharf to Cross the Huangpu River and Board the Ship at 10:00 This Morning. The Details Are Divided and Recorded on the Left.

Visiting Wang This Morning

At About 10:00 Yesterday Morning, Song Took a Car From His Residence to West Pubanshi Road and Visited Premier Wang Jingwei Again to Discuss the Matter of Attending the Washington World Economic Conference Again. Soon After, Vice Minister Liu Chongjie Also Arrived at Wang's Residence to Participate in the Discussion. Song Said Goodbye and Returned to His Residence at About 10:25. At This Point, the Negotiations Between Wang and Song Came to an End.

Documents Arrive in Shanghai

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Believes That Although the Washington Conference Is Mainly Focused on Economic Issues, It Is Closely Related to the Security Issues of Various Countries in the World. Therefore, All Relevant Documents Were Collected and Sent to Shanghai by Vice Minister Liu Chongjie. After Arriving in Shanghai Yesterday Morning, He First Went to Song's Residence to Deliver the Documents, and Then Went to Wang's Residence to Participate in the Discussion and Report on the Recent Diplomatic Situation to Wang.

Recent Photo of Song Ziwen

Receiving Guests

Important Figures Remaining in Shanghai All Believe That the Nature of the Conference Is Important, So They Have Visited Song One After Another to Say Goodbye and Discuss Attendance Opportunities. Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, and Yang Xingfo, Vice President, Visited With Xu Xinliu From the Banking Industry Yesterday Morning. Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, Also Visited in the Afternoon. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, and Others All Went to Say Goodbye.

Gathering and Discussion at the Kong Residence

Kong Xiangxi, the Newly Appointed President of the Central Bank, Invited Local Financial Giants to His Private Residence on West Aiams Road at 10:00 the Night Before Because Song Was About to Go Abroad to Discuss Everything. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, Wang Xiaolai, President of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and Shi Liangcai, a Leader in the Banking Industry, Were Present at the Time. They Discussed From 10:30 the Night Before Until 0:40 This Morning. It Is Said That the Content of the Meeting Was: (1) Regarding the Cases Proposed by Our Side for Song Treasurer to Attend the World Economic Conference Talks, (A) Tariff Issues, (B) Silver Price Issues, (C) Japanese Occupation of Various Customs Issues, (D) War Debt Issues, (E) Stopping the Violent Japan, Etc., Made Full Discussions to Contribute to Song's Preparations When Attending. (2) Regarding All Financial Issues After Song Treasurer Goes Abroad, It Is Said That the Results of the Consultation Were Extremely Satisfactory.

Visiting Song Qingling

Yesterday Afternoon, Song Went to 29 Moliai Road to Visit His Sister, Madam Sun Yat-sen, Song Qingling, to Say Goodbye. He Did Not Return Until 3:00 in the Afternoon. Later, Due to Days of Fatigue, He Took a Nap for a While. At About 5:00, He Went to the City Chamber of Commerce Again to Attend a Farewell Tea Party Held by Various Groups.

On Mr. Bei Songsun

Mr. Bei Songsun, the director of the Bank of China, is accompanying Mr. Song Ziwen to the United States this time to attend the Washington Economic Conference. A reporter from the New News Agency interviewed Mr. Bei yesterday.

Reporter (Q): Minister Song is taking you to the United States this time. Will you then proceed to London to attend the World Economic Conference?

(A): That has not been decided yet. We will make a final decision after arriving in the United States, depending on the needs of the situation.

(Q): How long do you plan to stay in the United States?

(A): Approximately two to three months. If we do not go to London, Minister Song will return to China first, and I will remain there temporarily to investigate the financial and economic situation in detail.

(Q): The United States is scheduled to convene a silver price conference in May. Do you intend to participate?

(A): The United States convenes silver price conferences from time to time, not just once in May, so I do not plan to participate.

Mr. Bei concluded by saying, "My trip to the United States with Minister Song this time is entirely from a business perspective. I will offer Mr. Song opinions on the suffering of the business community, hoping to establish a foundation for the recovery of our national economic prosperity."

Boarding This Afternoon

The President Jefferson of the Dollar Steamship Company, originally scheduled to set sail at 2:00 AM this morning, was rescheduled by the company to depart at 12:00 noon today due to Mr. Song's insufficient preparation time. According to reliable sources from the National News Agency yesterday, Mr. Song is scheduled to take a small boat prepared by the Customs from the New Customs Wharf at 10:00 AM today, sail to the center of the Yangshupu River, and board the President Jefferson.

In addition to the five people previously reported, including Yang Ge, Qin Fen, Huang Chundao, Bei Songsun, and Wei Wenbin, Mr. Cai Chousheng, a clerk from the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai Office, will also accompany them to the United States to serve as a telegram translator.

Various Groups Such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Joint Tea Party Farewell

More than 100 Representatives From All Walks of Life Attended

Mr. Song Gave a Sincere Speech on the Spot

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Local Cooperation Association, the Banking Association, the Money Trade Association, the General Labor Union, the Shipping Association, the Postal Workers Union, and other seven organizations held a farewell party at 4:00 PM yesterday in the main hall on the second floor of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to welcome Finance Minister Song Ziwen's attendance at the Washington Economic Conference. More than 100 people, including Song Ziwen and Wang Xiaolai, attended. The detailed records are as follows:

Representatives Attending

The representatives from various groups who attended yesterday included Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Yu Qiaqing, Wen Lanting, Lu Wenshao, Chen Yiting, Lao Jingxiu, Ma Shaoquan, Zhu Wenqi, Guo Shun, and Fang Jiaobo from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Li Fusun, Sun Jingxi, Wang Zhixin, Ye Fuxiao, Wu Yunzhai, Bei Lusun, Qu Jigang, Xu Xinliu, and Qian Xinzhi from the Banking Association; Qin Runqing and Pei Yunqing from the Money Trade Association; Shi Liangcai, Huang Renzhi, and Mu Ouchu from the Local Cooperation Association;

Du Yuesheng, Yang Zhixiong, and Hu Junzhuang, Du Chongyuan from the General Labor Union; Chen Peide, Lu Jingshi, and Zhu Xuefan from the transportation sector; Yan Renguang;

Wen Yuqing, Li Jingzong, and Zhu Ziqiao and Zha Liangzhao from the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association; Zhang Haian, the Jianghai Customs Superintendent; and more than 100 other people.

Chairman's Speech

Chairman Wang Xiaolai stood up and gave a farewell speech, the original text of which is of great importance.

A brief summary is recorded as follows: Minister Song, in his capacity as Deputy Dean of the Executive Yuan and concurrently Minister of Finance, left the country to participate in the World Economic Conference convened in Washington amidst the urgent situation. Our association, in view of the importance of this mission, is hosting this reception today to express our sincerity and expectations. Considering the current situation in our country, the so-called war debt issue and tariff issue, which are central to the economic conference, either have no direct relevance to our country, or are of secondary importance. The convening of this US economic conference has not invited even second and third-rate European countries, while our country, with its relatively shallow Far East ties and busy dealing with foreign troubles, is invited to the conference along with major European countries. This shows that the economic conference is a facade, and the content is certainly not so simple. The Japanese have seen through this and have made preliminary informal indications that the conference should not involve the Manchurian issue. However, the reason why the Japanese have been able to act wantonly in the Far East, occupying the four provinces and attacking Ludong, is that Europe and the United States are weakened by worker unemployment and war debt payment issues, and cannot effectively sanction Japan. Therefore, Japan sees this time as a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Therefore, if Europe and the United States want to interfere with Japan's atrocities, they must first adjust their internal affairs and gradually restore their vitality before taking effective action. Our country, as Europe and the United States' largest market in the Far East, needs them in this incident, and they also need us. We should do our best within the possible range to help alleviate the economic downturn in Europe and the United States, so that the task of this conference can achieve satisfactory results with our efforts, which will also have a positive impact on the Manchurian issue indirectly. This is called working hard here and reaping benefits there. This conference can be called a cadre conference of the great powers, and its importance may be above the Washington Conference of the Nine-Power Treaty in the past. How should our country make a sincere statement to move the world powers, so that they know that the world economic issue

cannot be separated from the Chinese economic issue, and the Chinese economic issue cannot be separated from the Northeast issue, so that they have a thorough understanding to change their Far East policy. This speech is far more effective than a public proposal. This is what we expect from Minister Song. Secondly, foreign troubles are increasingly urgent, and the task is heavy and arduous. It is up to you. The departure is imminent. We respectfully raise a glass to wish this trip success.

Representatives' Speeches

Representatives from various groups also delivered speeches in succession. The main points are recorded as follows: (1) Shi Liangcai said, "This World Economic Conference is extremely important. With Minister Song's position and reputation among friendly countries, it is natural that Minister Song should go in person. Therefore, at this farewell party, I hope that Minister Song can solve the domestic depression with fresh air after attending, and hope to achieve economic sanctions against Japan," etc. (2) Li Fusun briefly described the process of Minister Song's decision to attend the World Economic Conference, and then stated that with Minister Song's resolute spirit of abolishing the tael and changing the currency, he will surely be able to win many benefits after attending, and hopes that after returning to China, our country's economy and finance can open up a new life, or even find a solution to the Far East issue," etc. (3) Yu Qiaqing said, "China is now failing everywhere and being oppressed by others. If we can fight our way out of the economy, we can also defeat the enemy. After consolidating the economy, and then helping it with military force, there is no one who cannot win. Japan is only one-tenth of China, but it is called strong because it relies entirely on paper money and on the unity of its entire country. Therefore, if our country can unite and resist, it will surely have an advantage one day. Therefore, this time Minister Song is going to the United States to attend, on the one hand, hoping that the people of the whole country will cooperate with the government, and on the other hand, hoping that Minister Song can work hard for the country," etc. (4) Bei Songsun said, "This time I am following Minister Song abroad, as if in the position of a staff officer. In the past, our government's representatives to foreign countries have never had our merchants participate, but this time Minister Song actually came to find merchants, which shows that he is open-minded and can think for the people. The Minister of Finance has always been dedicated to raising funds, but Minister Song not only pays attention to handling finances, but also attaches great importance to the overall economic problem in the country. This is because he knows that the economic problem is actually the 'people's livelihood' mentioned by the Premier. The world's economic depression has now reached its extreme. At the convening of the China conference, our country must of course contribute its opinions to the conference, and it is very likely that the world will pay attention. Therefore, this conference is directly related to our industry and commerce. Minister Song invited me to participate and be consulted, and I am very willing to follow and contribute. However, I am afraid that my talents are limited, and there are many talented and knowledgeable people in our industrial and commercial circles. I am deeply afraid of failing to meet expectations," etc.

Mr. Song's Reply

After the representatives of various groups finished speaking, Minister Song stood up and replied, "I am very grateful to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Money Trade Association, and the Local Cooperation Association for their hospitality and farewell today. Mr. Li Fusun has just described the process of my decision to attend the Washington World Economic Conference.

However, when the United States invited our country, I was not prepared to attend because of the increasingly urgent internal and external troubles. After repeated urging from various parties and careful consideration, I felt that although this World Economic Conference is not directly related to the Far East issue, because of the mutual relationship and the entire world economic issue, I immediately decided to participate. In order to go to the United States quickly, I decided to leave tomorrow. As far as our country's current economy is concerned, the rural areas are bankrupt, commerce is declining, and currency is flowing into the cities, especially Shanghai. Productivity is declining day by day.

The reasons for this are the Yangtze River flood, the scourge of the Communist bandits, and Japan's economic invasion of our markets and military occupation of our four eastern provinces. These three points are all special difficulties that have arisen in our country as a result. However, the economic recession is a common phenomenon all over the world. It is not only our country that is like this. Even the United States, which is known as wealthy, is also unavoidable. Unemployed workers account for more than 15 million. In terms of population ratio, if you include their family members, the unemployed account for one-third. The United States is like this, and other countries can be imagined. Therefore, if we want to solve the domestic economic difficulties now, it is definitely not something that individual forces can do. If we build the Great Wall to close ourselves off, we must unite with all countries in the world to have hope. In the past, countries also tried to build the Great Wall in economic issues,

such as raising tariff barriers. Now they have realized that this is not the case. The central government sent me to attend this time because it wants to solve the domestic economic difficulties and must solve them together with the whole world. However, this trip is definitely not to ask for help, because China has a vast land and a population of 400 million, which is the world's largest market and will make a great contribution to the world in saving and solving the economic crisis. We can meet with all countries frankly, exchange opinions, and discuss solutions. Now that Japan is so barbaric, if our country only focuses on military force and does not work hard on the economy,

it is a mistake. A country is like a human body. It is definitely not healthy or fearless just by relying on the strength of one right arm. The entire body's functions must be fully utilized to be effective. Therefore, although this is an economic issue, it is also a national issue and a worldwide issue. Today, those who are seeing me off are all the elites from all walks of life. In the past, they have assisted me and overcome difficulties together.

I am grateful for their kindness, not only personally. After I board the ship tomorrow, I will stand in the position of the people. Therefore, although I am representing the government this time, I am also representing the people.

Whether this trip can live up to its mission depends entirely on the supervision and guidance of the government and the people. Therefore, after arriving in the United States, I hope to have telegrams to contribute opinions at any time and implement supervision. I will also report the detailed situation to you at any time." The meeting adjourned at about 6:00 PM.

Wang Jingwei Returned to Nanjing Last Night

Issued a Written Responsible Speech Before Leaving

Said that the Southwest Opposes the Entire Conference and is Difficult to Understand

Not Suppressing the Communist Bandits is Equivalent to Not Resisting Japan

Mr. Wang returned to Nanjing on the 11:30 PM express train last night because he had to attend today's administrative meeting. The railway bureau specially attached a flower car for Mr. Wang to ride in. Mr. Wang arrived at the station at 10:45 PM and went to bed because his back was hurting.

In addition to his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, those who traveled with him included Zeng Zhongming, Chen Gongbo, Jiao Yitang, Wang Zhengting, and Liu Ruiheng.

In addition, Ms. Soong Meiling, the wife of Chairman Jiang of the Military Affairs Commission, also went to Nanjing by night train last night. Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu is scheduled to return to Nanjing by early train this morning.

Mr. Wang issued a written statement yesterday, stating: (Q) The Southwest Central Committee members telegraphed on a cold day, still opposing the Central Committee's convening of a temporary national representative conference to discuss and decide on the early convening of the National Assembly. What are your thoughts on this? (A) The Southwest Central Committee members seem to have forgotten two things. First, the Fifth National Congress, according to the party constitution, must be held in November of this year. Now, holding a temporary national representative conference on July 1 is only a few months earlier. Second, the National Assembly, according to the decision of the Third Plenary Session, should be convened in April of the 24th year. Now, the so-called early convening is only a year and a half earlier. The Central Standing Committee, in view of the urgent national crisis, advocates early convening and has sufficient reasons, while their opposition seems not only to oppose early convening, but directly to oppose the convening of the National Congress and the National Assembly. It can be said that it is difficult to understand the interpreter.

(Q) Chairman Jiang's speech in Nanchang stated that during this serious period of suppressing the Communist bandits, advocating resistance against Japan should be strictly dealt with, which has aroused doubts from the outside world. What do you think, sir? (A) We must not take Chairman Jiang's speech out of context. Now, the task of the troops in North China is to resist Japan.

The task of the troops in Jiangxi is to suppress the Communist bandits. Both are contributing to the country and are equally important. However, if the troops in Jiangxi forget the current task of suppressing the Communist bandits and volunteer to resist Japan, it is tantamount to giving the Communist Party an opportunity to take advantage of. Therefore, Chairman Jiang cannot but repeatedly admonish them. Even more so, some people advocate that the troops suppressing the Communist bandits should be moved to resist Japan. Little do they know that the Communist bandits are still rioting in Jiangxi and other places during the serious national crisis.

This is tantamount to acting as an accomplice to the tiger. From this point of view, suppressing the Communist bandits is resisting Japan, and not suppressing the Communist bandits is equivalent to not resisting Japan. We must understand this point so that we do not misunderstand Chairman Jiang's speech.

Legal Rights and Administrative Integrity in Concessions

The Chinese Taxpayers Association Telegraphed the Authorities to Pay Attention

Preventing Concessions From Seizing Factory Management Rights

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association telegraphed Minister Luo of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Minister Luo of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing yesterday, (the title is omitted) stating: "Labor laws and regulations are laws that are enforced in our country's territory. No local agency may undermine them. Regardless of who has the police power in Shanghai, the management and inspection are solely the responsibility of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau from an administrative system perspective. The May 30th Massacre in the 14th year of the Republic of China, which opposed the Public Concession's Municipal Council's proposed amendment to Article 34 of the bylaws to include exchange printing and child labor, was also the biggest explosive. It has been nearly eight years since then, and our country's labor laws and regulations have been officially promulgated and implemented. However, the Municipal Council is actually trying to bring up the old matter again, planning to hold a special meeting on April 19, taking advantage of the annual meeting of taxpayers, to amend Article 34 of the bylaws in order to add the phrase "who has or occupies or opens a factory or workshop or engages in industry" under the phrase "within this boundary," so as to seize the power granted by the Central Government to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau,

and sever or undermine the integrity of our laws and regulations. The association did not dare to ignore the previous facts and current laws and regulations, and on April 12, at the representative conference of more than 96% of the residents within the boundary, it raised the case of the Municipal Council's proposed management of factories within the boundary. It was unanimously resolved, "According to the opinion of this conference, most of the workers in the factories in the Public Concession are our Chinese workers. If factory management and other laws and regulations are established in addition to the labor laws and regulations promulgated by our government, it will be detrimental to our country's sovereignty. Therefore, it is specially resolved that any motion or land charter and or amendment to the bylaws that grants the Municipal Council the power to manage, inspect, and or supervise all factories within the boundary will not be agreed to." The matter concerns the integrity of our country's legal rights and administration. It is reasonable to include a copy of the gazette, record the case, and telegraphically report it. Please investigate and act accordingly for the sake of the public. Chairman Wang Xiaolai and Xu Jilong of the Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association respectfully submit this telegram."

Yarn Merchants Selling Japanese Yarn

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Warns the Yarn Trade Association

The New Sound News Agency said, "The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Yarn Trade Association of this city, stating: 'It has been secretly reported that recently, yarn merchants such as Maochang, Ruixiang, Ruihe, Hemaom Beigongmao, Zhicheng, Baofeng, Zhenyuan, Xingsheng, Yifengxiang, Yitai, Fu Xiangji, Lin Yuanfeng, Zhang Jinji, Tongtaichang, Xingye Company, Maochang, Nangongmao, and various yarn shops in Xujiahui are selling Japanese yarn in large quantities without any scruples. Please find a way to stop them.' The case of economic severance with Japan has been resolved by the members' conference of this association after the September 18th Incident two years ago and notified to all industries to abide by it. Since then, Japanese goods should no longer be imported to show solidarity against the enemy. It is now reported that the industry is still selling Japanese goods as before, which is indeed contrary to the original plan of economic severance with Japan. The association, as a group of the same industry, cannot supervise and dissuade them at any time, and lets them act as they please, which is a loss of the status of the group and subject to criticism. A serious warning should be given. It is appropriate to enclose the original list and letter for investigation and strict prohibition." It is reported that the industry is now gathering to discuss the disposal method.

Unscrupulous Merchants Smuggle Japanese Fish and are Detained

Insane and Madly Pretending to be Domestic Products in an Attempt to Evade Taxes

Customs Detention and Punishment the Enemy Goods Inspection Association Asks for Severe Punishment

A telegram from the Shanghai Times News Agency reported that on the 13th of this month, there was a sand boat with the customs number of 0365 and the name Jinbaoli, the boat owner Zheng Quanliang, (that is, Ahao, according to the investigation of the Municipal Fishermen's Association, the boat had not come to Shanghai before) loaded yellow sand from Xiushan, Ningbo, and came to Shanghai, unloading at the Guangxin Wharf in Yangshupu. It finished unloading on the 14th, and then, at the request of a fishmonger surnamed Wang, it first sailed to Gaoqiao to load ice on the 15th, and then went to Bailonggang, Wusongkou, to smuggle more than 250 dan of small yellow croakers, large yellow croakers, and pomfrets from Japanese fishing boats, and sailed into the 16th Wharf in the early morning of the 17th for sale. The fishermen discovered their treachery, reported it to the Fish Industry Inspection and Enemy Goods Association, and reported it to the Customs. The Customs detained the ship because it falsely claimed to be domestic goods and attempted to evade national taxes (about 1,500 yuan). After investigation, the Fish Industry Inspection and Enemy Goods Association learned that this smuggling of Japanese fish was actually a pre-planned plan by Lu Jintang, the manager of Qiafeng, who was accustomed to doing business with Japanese fresh fish, and Wang Qingtang, a broker. Lu and others induced the unscrupulous merchants with cheap prices, as small yellow croakers have been cheap recently, only five or six yuan per dan, and the import tariff for Japanese ships is four yuan per dan. Therefore, Lu and others were blinded by greed and did everything possible, using this means of tax evasion to make profits. It is said that the unscrupulous merchants are still trying to dredge relations with the Customs, demanding exemption from punishment. The Customs, of course, cannot easily let them go, and the Fish Industry Inspection and Enemy Goods Association has also asked the higher authorities to investigate and punish them. At this time when the national crisis is at its height, the unscrupulous merchants dared to commit such an outrage, which is really insane and madly. It is hateful. Unless they are severely punished, it will not be enough to prevent future offenses.

Fourth Report on Aviation Fundraising Achievements

Totaling More Than 88,500 Yuan

The Japanese Danger in North China Requires National Salvation Without Delay

It Has Been Decided to Purchase Twelve Aircraft First to Go North to Resist the Enemy

The Chinese Aviation Association's fundraising team reported the fourth time's achievements yesterday, (the original scheduled date for the fourth report was the 15th, but it was postponed to yesterday due to the Western Spring Festival,) General Team Leader Wu Tiecheng hosted the leaders of the various fundraising teams at 4:00 PM on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, including Zhang Shouyong, Wang Xiaolai, Jin Liren, Dai Ji, Zheng Xigu, Li Tingan, Wen Hongen, Li Denghui, Tong Xingbai, Wu Xingya, Xu Peihuang, Xi Guansheng, Lin Wojiang, and more than 30 other people. General Team Leader Wu reported that the total achievement this time was 88,545 yuan, one dime, and five cents. Because the situation in North China is becoming more and more dangerous, the Aviation Association has decided to order twelve aircraft first.

Organize a team and go north to resist the enemy. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Summary of Speeches

Chairman Wu Tiecheng reported, briefly saying that today is the date for the fourth report on aviation fundraising achievements.

The total is only 88,545 yuan, and the total of the previous three times is less than one million. The distance from the planned goal of two million yuan is still far away, and it has been more than a month and a half since the fundraising began. There are only two weeks left until the end of April. We must redouble our efforts to achieve the goal. Recently, the situation in North China has become increasingly dangerous. Qinhuangdao, Beidaihe, etc. have all fallen into the hands of the enemy. Some people think that the country's affairs have reached this point, and aviation for national salvation is too late and does not help the actual situation. Little do they know that the Japanese's ambition will never be satisfied with just eastern Hebei. Therefore, it is increasingly urgent to establish an air force in the future. The Chinese Aviation Association originally planned to order aircraft after the fundraising in Shanghai ended. Now, because the national situation is critical, it has been decided to order twelve aircraft first, form an aviation team, and hand it over to the government to lead and go north to resist the enemy. Then Tong Xingbai gave a speech, saying that in terms of the fundraising process, those who eagerly donated are mostly from the lower and middle classes, while the wealthy who have huge sums of money are mostly reluctant to give even a hair. Recently, a car driver gathered more than 70 colleagues, each donating five yuan. The amount is indeed small and does not seem to be of much benefit, but the dedication of those who work hard to feed themselves to the country can be seen from this. On the other hand, those who are able to buy cars not only cannot donate to save the country like car drivers, but also often make remarks that confuse people, not exaggerating the enemy's power, saying that aviation for national salvation is of no avail, and even slandering the government, not resisting. Their hearts are really unbearable to ask. Then Li Denghui, Wen Yongshu, and others gave speeches in succession and dispersed.

Ningbo Aircraft

Two Stores Found to be Selling Inferior Goods Officially Announced

Welcome to Secretly Report Any Shortcomings to Help Rectify the Situation

The Nanjing Road Business Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens Association reported that the deadline for advising the few remaining stores selling inferior goods to voluntarily clean up their stock had passed yesterday. A meeting of the original personnel was convened yesterday morning for another secret inspection. Most stores were found to be genuinely pure. A few stores had suspicious items in their stock, and the sources needed to be investigated further to determine right from wrong. However, Tong Chenchang Foreign Goods Store at the eastern end of Bentang Lane and the Chinese store diagonally opposite Wangping Street made verbal promises but continued to openly display and sell large quantities of inferior cotton and wool knitwear. Therefore, the association has jointly decided to formally publish a report in the next day or two, detailing the situation of each store on the road regarding the presence of inferior goods. This will allow consumers to know where to go and what to avoid, with the intention of rewarding good behavior and punishing bad, thereby inspiring patriotism. It is also heard that the association welcomes reports from all sectors at any time, but they must be accompanied by concrete evidence to supplement the shortcomings of the association's inspectors.

Another Bomb Explodes at Juchang Cotton Cloth Store

Around 7 PM Last Night Near Bulin Lane

Doors and Windows Shattered, But No One Injured

Juchang Cotton Cloth Store (specializing in wholesale foreign cloth and textile trade), located at No. 140-142 Bulin Lane, west end of Zhengjia Wood Bridge Street in the middle section of Avenue Dubail (Gongguan Road), is a double-fronted store opened by several shareholders, with Ma Yulong from Ningbo serving as a shareholder and manager. Business has been quite prosperous. At around 7 PM yesterday (the 17th), while the shop assistants were having dinner in the inner hall, a bomb suddenly flew in from the middle of the road, causing a loud explosion that shook the neighborhood. Smoke filled the air. Fortunately, there were no customers in the store at the time, and the shop assistants were all in the inner hall. Only several pieces of door and window glass were shattered, and no one was injured. When the patrolling police heard the sound and arrived, the bomber had already disappeared. The head of the French Concession Police Department dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate, and they collected the bomb fragments from the ground and took them back to the police station pending investigation and the arrest of the bomber.

Municipal Government to Announce Housing Lease Regulations

Approved by the Executive Yuan

The city has a vast area, a large population, and expensive housing prices, so residents often have to rent. In order to facilitate residents' housing leases and avoid disputes, the municipal government previously drafted the Shanghai Housing Lease Regulations and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for review. The Executive Yuan entrusted the Ministry of Interior to review the regulations, made some minor revisions, and then resubmitted them to the Executive Yuan. The municipal government received instructions from the Executive Yuan on the morning of the 17th, approving the record. Therefore, the regulations will be announced soon.
