Great China University Wins Jiangnan University Basketball Championship

▲ Won Again in the Second Final Against Jinan with a Score of 41 to 26

▲ The Situation Was Tense, Jinan Lost Ground in the Last Ten Minutes Due to Heavy Pressure

Great China University won this year's Jiangnan University Basketball Championship. In yesterday's second final against Jinan, Great China won again by a large margin of 41 to 26. This is the first time that Great China University has won the Jiangnan University Basketball Championship. Last year's competition was not held due to the Shanghai War. The previous champion was Chizhi. Great China hosted a banquet last night to reward the championship team. The situation of yesterday's second final is as follows:

Great China's Arrogant Momentum

Several seconds after the referee Li Zuqi blew the whistle, Great China jumped and got the ball. Chen Shiqiu charged to the basket and scored with a swoop. Jinan's Xu Rongshui scored a point with a free throw. Great China's Guan Dang'an attacked from behind, and Ren Jiexing made a wonderful shot. After these two goals, Great China was leading by 6 to 1, with arrogant momentum. The cheering students raised their voices.

Jinan Tries Hard to Catch Up

Seeing the fierce momentum, Jinan called a timeout to temporarily blunt their attack. Yu Wencai, Xu Rongshui, and Wang Nanzhen successively made contributions, changing the score from 6 to 3, 8 to 5, and then to an equal 8 to 8. The situation changed. Han Zhenyuan's goal even put Jinan ahead by two points. This was the golden age of Jinan. Ren Jiexing's two hits put Great China ahead again by 14 to 10, leading by four points. Yin Guiren refused to give in, scoring one point with a free throw and one point with a long shot. The result of the first half was 14 to 13, with Great China winning over Jinan by one point.

The Situation Remains Tense

The first half passed in an extremely tense situation. The battle resumed in the second half, and there was still no relaxation. Ren Jiexing and Chen Shiqiu scored continuously, and Yin Guiren and Xu Rongshui also retaliated, still seeing the equal score of 17 to 17. Great China's Guan Dang'an was fouled out for the fourth time, making the score 21 to 18. Jinan began to lag behind by three points. Great China did not waver due to Guan's expulsion, and the attack became even more fierce, and the situation took a sharp turn.

The Battle Situation Takes a Sharp Turn

After 21 to 18, Great China began to make vigorous progress. Jinan fought hard to defend, but the formation eventually crumbled. Ren Jiexing hit three out of three shots, making the score 25 to 18, then 32 to 20, 36 to 26. The score difference hovered around ten points. Great China added another five points, and the game ended with a final score of 41 to 26.

Great China Was Slightly Better

Yesterday's performance was better than the first final, the panic was slightly reduced, and the situation was tense all the way until the end when the outcome was decided. In terms of skill, Great China was better than Jinan, being more familiar and accurate. Ren Jiexing's shooting was the best. Jinan was slightly unskilled and slow.

Unable to find opportunities under the basket, Yin Guiren's long shots created a lot for Jinan.

Securities

Government Bonds Extremely Weak

Various Prices Fall Again by 3-4 Jiao to 1 Yuan

Yesterday, although the price fluctuations on the Chinese Securities Exchange were not significant, the trend was quite simple. Because Qinhuangdao was again declared lost, the market sentiment was extremely weak. Fortunately, the Guangdong group not only did not sell, but also slightly replenished their holdings.

At the opening in the morning, the market sentiment was quite tense, with most advocating selling.

For a time, the quantity of supply and demand was quite disparate, and the market price fell by several jiao from the 18 mark. Afterwards, there was a trend of supply exceeding demand in all items. No. 50 sold particularly heavily, so the downward trend intensified after the entry of sellers. The customs tax fell by about 1 yuan. However, because the large investors remained cautious and took no action, the closing and afternoon trading both entered a state of anxiety, indicating that the short sellers did not dare to be bold.

Because the situation is changing extremely rapidly, especially as the settlement period approaches, there are many dangers. From the slight rebound of two or three jiao at the morning closing and the mixed ups and downs in the two afternoon sessions, it can be seen that people are uneasy and have no definite grasp. As a result, market prices fell by three or four jiao to one yuan. If the war does not extend to Tianjin and Hebei, market prices may rebound, and caution is necessary. The total transaction volume was 8,311,000 yuan, of which only 1,000 yuan was in spot goods, with futures and forward contracts accounting for two-thirds and recent contracts accounting for one-third. Among the various transactions, the consolidated customs tax accounted for the majority, totaling 3,265,000 yuan, military cuts accounted for 1,190,000 yuan, and the 19 mark accounted for 1,025,000 yuan, with the rest ranging from tens of thousands to 700,000 to 800,000.

Bean Flour Market Re-Enters Sluggish Path

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month was in a stable state. As a result, this month was down 0.25 li compared to the previous day, May was down 0.5 li, June was down 0.75 li, July was down 0.25 li,

August was up 0.25 li, and September was down 0.5 li.

A Glimpse of the Decline of the Wheat Bran Market

The wheat bran market has been in a sluggish state for a long time. Because domestic sales have gradually disappeared, it is due to the economic bankruptcy of the rural areas and the unwillingness of domestic and foreign traders to extend credit, so the decline of the market is becoming more and more serious. Most of the factory's inventory is still handled by the hostile merchants, and a small portion is sold to Fujian, Xiamen, and Shantou. The inland groups are unusually quiet.

Recently, the factory price has fallen to 1.55 yuan with a discount.

Car Beans Slightly Better, Red Grain Sales Active

Yesterday, the car bean market was slightly better. Because the cargo owners have suffered too much loss, the downstream transport is sluggish, so the source is temporarily disconnected. Sugar Market: Coarse Granulated White Sugar Weak

Domestic Brown Sugar Slightly More Advantageous

Yesterday, the sugar market's benchmark price remained unchanged. Due to sluggish sales, market sentiment continued to be weak. The No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar from the association was quoted at $21.20,

while the No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was at $20.06, with no transactions. The No. 8 and 9 Dutch brown sugar had some trading, with prices at $17 to $16.95. Domestic new cotton brown sugar arrived yesterday from Suzhou via two shipments totaling thousands of packages.

On the same day, Chaozhou merchants offered over two hundred packages, with prices ranging from $16.25, $16.20, $16.10 to $15.95.

Sales were relatively active. Hainan brown sugar sold over a hundred packages from Guangdong merchants, with prices at $14.60. Due to low inventory, the market was also firm.

Cloth and Wool Market: Quiet and Desolate

Transactions of cloth and wool were very quiet at the association. Demand from various domestic merchants was minimal, as business for retailers was slow and market sales were quite stagnant. Additionally, the approaching end of the month for long-term payments caused tight credit among the industry, with both buyers and sellers eager to liquidate goods for cash. Market prices consequently declined steadily. Currently, the wholesale and retail prices of spring and summer wool fabrics are lower than before, but actual large-scale transactions are rare.

Overall, the market trend yesterday showed a sharp downward turn.

Metals: Zinc Increased in Line with Fixed Prices

Due to frequent increases in overseas fixed prices, the local standard price of zinc has also risen. The current fixed price is $38.75, an increase of $1.00 from before. The Shanghai market has also increased to $16.50, up by $0.50 from before. Trading among tea merchants was vigorous, and demand from paint companies and yellow lead factories was also strong. However, export business to Tianjin, Qingdao, and Yantai was affected by the ongoing war in the north.

There was no progress in transactions. Merchants from Changjiang Road and Fujian-Zhejiang areas slightly increased their orders. The market supply is shallow, with few goods arriving, so the outlook for future prices is relatively optimistic.

Pure Antimony: Arrival of Spot Goods

Recently, the market in Hunan for pure antimony has been calm, and exports have increased sharply, resulting in a large number of spot goods arriving in Shanghai. Last week's arrivals were particularly high,

totaling 40 to 50 tons. As a result, supply exceeded demand, and the market was sluggish.

The standard price appeared strong externally but was weak internally, selling for $335 per ton, a decrease of over $2 from before. However, retail transactions could still barely fetch $336. Besides minor demand from enamel factories and manufacturers, export business was virtually non-existent. According to Reuters, Russia and Canada are producing large quantities of pure antimony, and European and American markets are mostly occupied. Therefore, apart from Japan, there is no foothold for Chinese goods overseas, making a turnaround in the local market seem difficult.

White Lead Skins: New Goods Arrive

Due to a shortage of goods, the market price of white lead skins has risen sharply. Types like No. 2 and No. 5 were particularly scarce, leading to higher prices. Subsequently, purchasers could hardly find goods available. Yesterday, 400 to 500 barrels arrived via the New Taikoo Wharf, easing concerns about market shortages.

Silk and Tea

News of New Anhui and Zhejiang Tea

Since the Qingming Festival, the tea buds in the mountains around Sui'an for green tea have gradually grown larger. Generally, tea farmers, noting last year's good prices for early buds, plan to start picking earlier this year. It is expected that this year's tea production from this area will be of high quality.

Tea shops have also been busily preparing to open for the season, and tea merchants from various regions have been very active, creating an unusually lively atmosphere.

Decrease in Tunxi Tea Firms

Tunxi is an important area for the Anhui tea market. Last year, most tea businesses in this area suffered losses, so tea merchants are not very active this year. Currently, over ten tea firms in Tunxi have decided to cease operations. The remaining forty-eight firms are still operating as usual, but most are adopting a cautious approach.

Free Talk

On Spring Outings

— Yu Dafu

The good thing about spring is that people don’t feel like eating much; the bad thing about spring is that people don’t feel like doing much. "Drowsy and dreaming all day," this is the spirit of spring. When drunk and dreaming, one naturally doesn't feel like eating or doing things, but there are exceptions. The gluttonous man of Qi, who begged for food between meals, is an exception that can break this rule. In short, spring is not for studying. With spring clothes ready and spring emotions stirring, outings and tomb sweeping, fulfilling vows and offering incense, seem to be the only proper things to do in spring. Li Bai's preface to the spring night banquet in the peach and plum garden truly captures the psychology of spring. The philosophy of decadent Chinese poets can be seen in this short preface.

However, Li Bai was not just a poet who peddled decadence. In his preface to the night banquet on Tiger Hill on the fifteenth day of the twelfth month, he also explained the reasons for his decadence: "Now, within the court, there are Kui, Long, Gao, and Yi to assist in all affairs of state. Outside, there are Fang Shu and Zhao Hu to defend the four corners of the land. People by the rivers and seas can rest easy and have nothing to worry about. Thus, we can enjoy banquets with friends, playing music and drinking wine, and compose poems under the bright moon. This is the duty of our group..." Looking back at the current situation in China, what is it like? But distant fires seem to never burn the water nearby. The flames of war in North China are, of course, irrelevant to us. Therefore, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau can open special spring excursion trains, and movie queens can hold all-night dance parties.

Speaking of outings, they are not inherently bad. The "Monthly Commands" chapter of the Book of Rites says: "In the middle month of summer, one can look far into the distance and climb mountains and hills." Moreover, Confucius traveled north, sighed deeply, and urged his disciples to each express their aspirations. The Grand Historian traveled to famous mountains and great rivers, and his writings were thus accomplished. In medieval Germany, apprentices who completed their apprenticeship had to travel to broaden their horizons. Therefore, after the apprenticeship period (LEHRJAHRE), there was a mandatory period of travel (WANDERJAHRE). This kind of travel is a rewarding journey, a decoration to peaceful times, and should not be criticized. However, given the current state of China, with starving corpses in the suburbs and flames of war everywhere, the question remains whether the idle and propertied classes should be so wasteful.

Although, one can not forget to save the country while enjoying spring, and one can not forget to enjoy spring while saving the country, but is this really true?

On Daze Village

— Cao Juren

"Daze Village," "Leopard Head Lin Chong," and "Stone Tablet" are three short stories that Mao Dun wrote in the style of "new wine in old bottles." I think "Stone Tablet" is more successful, while Mao Dun himself feels that "Daze Village" "appears more intimate" (see my "Reminiscences," page 8). "Daze Village" is originally a good subject matter, but Mao Dun's observations are not very accurate; I don't think it should be written that way.

The characters from the Chu-Han Contention can be divided into three groups:

Fan Zeng, Lu Jia, Song Yi, Zhang Liang, and Xiao He make up one group, representing the scholar-official class. Their policy was, "It is better to belong to someone. If things succeed, you can still be ennobled; if things fail, it is easy to escape, and you will not be known by the world." They had a common goal of establishing lords to rally support. Tian Shi, Tian An, Tian Rong, Han Guang, Zhao Wang Xie, and Chu Wang Xin make up another group, representing the fallen gentry. They relied on the scholar-officials' dream of restoring their countries. Xiang Ji, Xiang Liang, Liu Ji, Chen Sheng, Wu Guang, Han Xin, and Peng Yue make up yet another group, representing the rogue class. They were the central figures of that era, each harboring the ambition of "I can take his place." Surrounding these three groups were millions of farmers, whose grievances had been building up and were ready to explode. The rogue class took advantage of this accumulated resentment and seized the opportunity to launch a rebellion.

"Daze Village" is a good subject matter because it can represent the way of peasant revolutions for thousands of years.

The uprising in "Daze Village" was not sudden; it had been planned beforehand. Chen She was an ambitious man who, when farming in his hometown, made promises of "If I become rich, I will not forget you." He knew that his opportunity had come with the rain in "Daze Village." He "falsely claimed that Prince Fusu and Xiang Yu were singing for the world," "placed a silk cloth with writing in the belly of a fish," and "lit bonfires at night and howled like a fox." These were all the tactics of a conspirator and not the consciousness of poor farmers. Mao Dun seems to have overlooked this point. He treated Chen She as an ordinary farmer, and therefore shifted the focus to the two drunken officers, making the shadow very faint.

When writing historical novels, one can certainly inject new meaning, but it should not deviate too much from historical facts. The peasant revolution in "Daze Village" contained two kinds of consciousness: one was the resistance of the poor farmers against the nobles, and the other was the resistance of the Chu people against the Qin people. Let's look at the scholar-official class at that time, who all spoke of establishing a Chu ruler. This kind of national consciousness certainly had a rallying power for the farmers at that time. It was not until Liu Ji and Xiang Yu took the center stage as the rogue class that the national resistance sentiment declined. When writing about "Daze Village," if these two kinds of consciousness are not properly interwoven, as Mao Dun did by only writing about one kind of consciousness, it will obscure the truth of the matter. In Chinese peasant revolutionary movements, the peasants are often unconscious, so they are often taken advantage of by others. The "Biography of Chen She" in the Records of the Grand Historian clearly says, "The soldiers often talked among themselves, all pointing at Chen Sheng. Wu Guang was always kind to people, and many soldiers were willing to work for him." This is clear evidence of the successful exploitation of farmers. But Mao Dun says, "However, they were only surprised.

They had no illusions. They had already tasted enough of the idea of supporting someone as 'king.' All they hoped for was to break the chains that bound them." This is definitely not the Chinese peasant, and even less so the Chinese peasant of that time. Writing it this way cuts off the link between the rogue class and the peasants.

There are many other scattered opinions that I will not write down. I now want to try to fill a new wine into the old bottle.

"We Can Wait Fifty Years"

— Yang Xingzhi

Not long ago, Dr. Hu Shih, a "high-class Chinese," wrote an article in "Independent Review" advocating direct negotiations with Japan. Except for "certain conditions," the goal of the negotiations should be: "To abolish the puppet state of Manchukuo and restore China's territorial and administrative sovereignty over the three northeastern provinces and Jehol." But why should this be the goal? "The reason is very simple," namely, "First, we must be consistent with the League of Nations and the United States' 'non-recognition doctrine'; second, we should not abandon the League of Nations."

Dr. Hu's proposal is certainly clever. First, he can use the four words "direct negotiations" to completely eliminate the national revolutionary war of resisting Japanese imperialism. Second, he can use the four words "certain conditions" to sell the entire Chinese nation as pigs and dogs. Third, he cleverly uses "being consistent with the League of Nations and the United States" as a footnote to "the goal of negotiations should be to abolish the puppet state of Manchukuo and restore China's territorial,

and administrative sovereignty over the three northeastern provinces and Jehol." This means that it doesn't matter if our country is conquered, but we must be consistent with our masters, because our masters have not told us to recognize Manchukuo, and we still have many things to rely on our masters for, and we must not break away from their embrace.

In this way, all Chinese people below our group of "high-class Chinese" will understand the principle of "masters first, nation second," and from then on, they will all bow their heads and listen quietly to the orders of their masters, and wait quietly to be slaughtered by their masters. Ah, we should thank Dr. Hu for his revelation and his plan.

However, this clever plan has now failed. Based on "experimentalism," this plan has already failed, first because the "lower-class Chinese" still dare to not allow the government authorities to act as Li Hongzhang today, and second because, according to Japanese Minister to China Arima, "Now that Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, if China and Japan negotiate directly,

it will invisibly raise China's international status," clearly "disdaining" to negotiate directly with China. In this way, our doctor's clever plan has failed.

What does it matter if it fails? Let's try another one. In short, we must not allow an anti-Japanese national revolutionary war. Since Japan does not allow us to negotiate, we should "wait for death." So our doctor shouted in the 44th issue of "Independent Review," "We can wait fifty years!"

What is the meaning of "waiting fifty years"? First, of course, it is still not allowed to move, not allowed to resist. Second, it is only allowed to watch Manchukuo being established, not allowed to "recover." Third, it is allowed to let the Japanese take whatever they want. For fifty years, or perhaps for an infinite number of years, we are not allowed to move. Being a slave means being a slave for a lifetime.

Because "the support of righteousness in the whole world is on our side, and the moral condemnation of the whole world is on the heads of our enemies." This means that the masters are also not very satisfied with Japan's "exclusive possession" of Manchuria, and at the same time they are very satisfied that we are willing to be slaughtered and have no resistance at all. Therefore, "our final victory is beyond any doubt." Final victory, okay, we just need to have this little bit of "confidence." Doesn't it matter what we do? What does fifty years matter? Our days as slaves are still long!

Mr. He Jiagan wrote in a poem, "A parrot that can speak is as poisonous as a snake." I think our "parrot" is "clever" because he can make a clever footnote to "long-term resistance," he can make a better reassurance pill, he can make a more ingenious smoke screen. Ah, our parrot, our doctor, our high-class Chinese!

However, I heard that recently Yosuke Matsuoka went from Geneva to Washington to lobby the United States to place China under joint control. Therefore, former U.S. Undersecretary of State Cassel attributed the new interpretation of the Stimson Doctrine. Former U.S. Department of Commerce Far East Director Adler even publicly advocated that the three northeastern provinces should be governed by Japan. From this point of view, the masters seem to have changed their minds and seem to be planning to divide the spoils peacefully with Japan. What should we do then? Ah, our doctor, our living treasure.

On the Way Home (Continued)

— Liu Zeng

The Longhua Pagoda, which I haven't seen for many years, is now very beautiful in my eyes, clearly depicted on the thin background of the painting. Three years ago, on a similarly drizzly spring afternoon, I wandered alone in Parc de Laeken, a suburb of the Belgian capital. I thought the Japanese tower built there was also quite unique and lingered to admire it for a long time. Now, facing this handsome Longhua Pagoda, the Japanese tower in my memory seems a little short and clumsy.

Qingming has just passed, and new soil has been added to many tombs along the road. Previously, these kinds of things would not have attracted my attention. Even if I noticed them, I would have felt some disgust. But now it is different, because the person I love the most has also entered this world, so even the unrelated mounds of other people's graves seem to have some connection with me, and I look at them with kind and affectionate eyes.

The car passed through a small stream. Along the stream, rows of peach and willow trees, which just a few days ago had only some green buds on their branches, are now colorful and dressed in charming spring clothes. A few fast-growing willow trees already have slender branches swaying in the wind.

The further the car travels away from the city, the more peach and willow trees are sent from the fields and vegetable plots. Sometimes you can even see dozens or hundreds of neatly arranged peach orchards, but the densely packed flowers in full bloom are so vulgar red that they are unpleasant to look at. It is better to have only willow trees with green leaves, which appear simple and lovely.

Speaking of willow trees, they are truly the most poetic and picturesque plants. In Europe, although willow trees are not often seen, the words "SAUIE" and "WILLOW" in Western languages are like "yang liu" in Chinese, often seen in poems. When my wife was alive, she loved to recite Musset's famous work:

My dear friends, when I am dead,

Please plant a willow tree on my grave.

I love its tearful, dense branches and leaves,

The pale color makes me feel dear and tender.

It will also have light shadows

Covering the desolate hill where I lie.

Now that the willow is green and the person is gone, recalling Musset's poem alone in the car is like my wife speaking. The past is like a dream, how can I not weep!

I don't know when two foreign young men came up into the car, with thin faces and tall statures, they looked like Englishmen. It is rare for this city bus to carry a few foreigners in a year, and the appearance of these two white men caused surprise among many small merchants and landlords in the car. Everyone stared at them intently, murmuring and talking. (To be continued)

Full-Length Novel

The Crossroads of Era and Love

— Zhang Ziping

He decided to go to the publishing house organized by Li Yixiang and Chen Huamin to see those literary friends and inquire about the news of the comrades who were arrested this afternoon. The publishing house was located in Hongkou, within the sphere of influence of Japanese imperialism. It would take at least an hour to get there from here. But Haiquan, who had nowhere to go tonight, decided to go there to spend the night.

When he arrived at their publishing house, it was already half past eight. Most of the partners in the publishing house had gone out to play. Only two or three less important staff members were still there reading or scribbling. Haiquan had been there several times and knew them, so he greeted them. But they were cold and didn't pay much attention to Haiquan. Haiquan asked them where Mr. Li Yixiang lived, and they all said they didn't know. He then asked if Mr. Li would come here tonight, but they didn't give a definite answer. Haiquan felt bored and just flipped through the newspapers in the reading room and looked at the social science books they published. He looked until nine thirty and was about to go back to Cao Shiguang's house when he suddenly heard a burst of footsteps in the corridor outside.

"I'm afraid they're going to come and search. It's best to be more mature."

"There's no problem, right?"

Haiquan clearly heard Mr. Chen Huamin's voice.

"What are you afraid of? What are you afraid of? There's no such barbaric way!"

This time it was Mr. Li Yixiang's voice.

"But imperialists don't reason."

"There's nothing in our society anyway. Let them come and check! They won't seal us up. No matter what, they won't be so barbaric."

Haiquan came out to see that behind Mr. Chen and Mr. Li were also four or five second- or third-rate writers. Haiquan couldn't help but envy this group of famous writers. They all sat down in the living room. Haiquan also came in, first called out to Li Yixiang, and then nodded to Chen Huamin and called him Mr. Chen.

"Ah, you've come."

Li Yixiang seemed surprised to see Haiquan.

"Mr. Li, how did you escape back?"

Haiquan asked with a smile.

"Joke! Why escape? Would those police officers dare to arrest people randomly?"

Talk

Nude Dance

— Tianfang

I have always had a preference when reading newspapers, which is to read the advertisements before reading the news. The first, of course, is to see if there are any new books published, and the second is to know a little about the methods of publicly scolding people, such as you say I take bribes, I accuse you of slander, or reveal some of other people's secrets as evidence that my goods are genuine and of good quality. Because I have paid the money, I can speak much more freely and happily, which is more truthful and revealing than the news reported by interviewers.

This is my reason for liking to read advertisements.

Recently, this preference seems to be even greater. The reason is also very simple: the pages are filled with "national salvation," "resolutions," "telegrams," and "new Chen lines," which have made me a little tired. Although a certain general told us that "internal worries and external troubles are not to be feared,"

this heart is still quite uneasy, probably a sign of "being dead."

Yesterday, as usual, I flipped through the newspapers one by one, and in the advertisements for "engagement," "obituary," and "denial of slander," I found the following advertisement, which I hereby transcribe for public viewing:

Our theater has been overcrowded since the screening of XXX and the French nude dance, and we have been unable to accommodate all the viewers. Every show has had over a thousand people turned away. Our theater feels very sorry for this. Viewers are requested to arrive early to avoid disappointment.

Although this is an advertisement, and the purpose is perhaps mainly to encourage people to "arrive early," the crowding of the audience is at least half true. Since the "artistic traitor" Liu and the "commander-in-chief of the five-province allied forces" Sun handled the nude negotiations, this trend has become very popular. The eyes of ordinary people are not on the beauty of art, but only seek the nudity of the "jade body," which may be an expression of "dogs grabbing carpets." As for "dancing," it is even more impossible without "nudity," let alone "nuding" a "beautiful and young" "French woman," so its popularity is self-evident. It also contains the meaning of respecting imported goods.

What is "apologetic" is that every show has "no less than a thousand" "viewers" turned away, craning their necks outside the venue, wanting to get close to the "beauty" but unable to do so. Seeing this is truly pitiful, so not only the theater owner feels "sorry," but even the newspaper reader feels injustice on their behalf. Here, I can't help but feel that the great wish to "sacrifice beauty" is still limited by material things, which should be improved by the theater owners who are responsible for promoting "aesthetic artification." Fortunately, there are so many dance troupes now, truly no less than "mushrooms after rain," and they are all "beautiful and young," and although they are not "French," many are "foreign-born" and all are willing to "sacrifice their beauty." "Fat buttocks tremble, endlessly changing, able to melt the soul of Liu Hui: Curves are slightly presented, enough to intoxicate the souls of men from Lu. Looking at their bodies makes people dizzy and confused, their hearts swayed and their minds extinguished; being near them is like the fragrance of musk orchids, making people limp and weak..." (original text from a certain theater advertisement, author's annotations). Just seeing this advertisement is enough to make people "float," and the "satisfaction" is roughly the same. There is no shortage of "beautiful and young" women, and as long as you make a grand wish, anyone can be nude and be welcomed in the same way, so the supply is not likely to cause a major panic, which is reassuring. Finally, I would like to take this opportunity to post a free advertisement on behalf of major theaters. I guarantee with my reputation that this is indeed the only anesthetic for people in semi-colonial countries under the heavy oppression of imperialism. If you have already written a "confession" of "never resisting," then it is very worthwhile to spend a few dimes to "arrive early" |late will "disappoint" | in order to vent the anger in your stomach.

Random: The affairs of the country are so muddled, why don't I seek happiness?

The booming of the cannons, how can it be as pleasant as Pina's voice?

Since the passing of Xia Yu, the nude country can still be found;

May the "beauty" be always close, why bother to value the past and despise the present?

The Abrogation of Taels and Adoption of Yuan: An Abacus Tactic

— Luo Zhensheng

Since April 6th, with the abrupt implementation of abolishing taels and adopting yuan, all silver transactions must be calculated using 0.715 as the exchange rate. This is especially cumbersome for those working in the financial sector. I have now devised a quick method to share with readers. Although some have already published on this, this method is still incomplete. If one can practice it thoroughly, it is much more convenient than repeatedly dividing by 0.715. I will provide specific examples below:

Convert 1,000 taels into yuan: Multiply by 1.4, resulting in 1,400 yuan. Then, in the fourth position from the right, subtract 14, yielding 1,398 yuan and 6 jiao. For values like 10,000, 100,000, 1 million, or 10 million taels, add 13,986 in the seventh position from the right, then skip seven positions and add 13,986 again, rounding to the nearest fen. It is perfectly accurate. For instance, to convert 15,000 taels, multiply by 1.4, obtaining 21,000 yuan. Subtract 12 in the fourth position from the right, resulting in 20,979 yuan and 2 fen. By extrapolating from this and practicing diligently, it will be faster than repeatedly dividing by 0.715. Gentlemen, why not give it a try?

(Principle) Converting 100 taels to yuan using 0.715 yields 139 yuan, 8 jiao, and 6 fen. Adding 14 to the fourth position results in 140 yuan. Extrapolating from this, multiply the original value in taels by 1.4, then subtract the number obtained by multiplying by 14 from the fourth position from the right. This yields the equivalent amount in yuan. If the silver amount is in the tens of thousands, add the obtained yuan amount to the seventh position from the right (rounding). If the silver amount is in the tens of millions, skip another seven positions and add the yuan amount again. (Gratitude)

Literature and Art

Wandering Poet Immortal (Continued)

— Qian Mengqiao

The immortal's banner guards the imperial court,

All under heaven revere the spirit of King Jiang.

Ascend the altar not to expound the "Can Tong Qi,"

But to beg for the "Huang Ting" and "Dun Jia" scriptures.

There is a telegram proposing to promote Jiang to Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force.

The elixir talisman is deeply hidden in the Shangqing residence,

An edict forbids weapons from leaving the Jade Threshold.

Ultimately, he who tied the bell must untie it himself,

The cave gate receives the five thunder scriptures.

Britain cancels the embargo on arms,

Supporting half of the rivers and mountains.

Riding a mythical bird, he comes and goes in the green mist,

One can know that he who scatters beans to create soldiers,

Is not a spirit official but a wandering immortal.

Referring to General Zhu Ziqiao

He brushes his sleeves and returns to the peak on the sea,

The immortal alliance has disappointed a sentimental person.

The Shangyuan Palace reopens the banquet,

The Grand Duke in the East has vanished without a trace.

Japan withdraws from the League of Nations.

The calamity burns Kunming into ashes,

After the mulberry fields change, they belong to Penglai.

Knowing well it is not the Eastern King's enterprise,

One must wait for the Celestial Dragon to demand it back.

After the European War, the League of Nations entrusted Japan with the trusteeship of Pacific Islands. Now, they will demand it back.

He returns to tie his horse on Langfeng Peak,

How many years since our separation from the jade palace?

Once, he was the azure bird messenger of Pengshan,

Do not let him secretly deliver love letters.

Former Japanese Ambassador to China, Yoshizawa, visits China.

A Trip to West Lake?

— Kuang Bei

It's already the third month of late spring. Young men and women escaping the confines of steam-heated rooms are eager to try on their 1933 spring attire and stroll into the countryside to appreciate the scenery. Life is always so harmonious, fresh, lively, and lovable. It's said that the spring scenery of Jiangnan is exceptionally captivating. "Spring grass green, spring water green waves" are elegant lines from the ancients. And "Late spring, third month, Jiangnan grass grows, various flowers bloom on trees, a flock of orioles flies wildly" is an even more vivid depiction. Yes, "Face the wine, sing a song, how long is life?" Why not seize the moment and have a good time? The ancients even had the refined pastime of "holding a candle to wander at night." Are we really going to let even the daytime pass in vain?

I hear that "West Lake Madness" has been all the rage for weeks. In the spring of Jiangnan, West Lake is indeed uniquely beautiful. Having roamed the seas for a full five years, I have long been deeply impressed by it, and I often yearn for the tomb by the lake—that of Master Manshu, the author of "Broken Geese and Lost Swans." But I have never been there in person.

This time, this year, Mr. X started trying to get train tickets from the railway bureau half a month ago. I also rashly agreed to accompany him. Time flies like a shuttle. Last night, Mr. X came to tell me that the tickets were secured and that we would leave early on the 17th. He asked if I had prepared a few yuan for spending money. I suddenly woke up from a deep dream and blurted out that I wasn't going. I truly regret disappointing Mr. X. Is it because I can't scrape together a few yuan? Not at all! It's already late spring, and the weather is turning warm. I can simply roll up the bedding on the bed and send it to the pawnshop. Even if it doesn't fetch five or ten yuan, three yuan would be enough. That way, I wouldn't have to beg others and be met with a nose full of ashes, with a barrage of excuses like, "Difficult, difficult, it's really difficult right now. If you wait a few more days, maybe I can come up with something."

So why am I not going? I just feel that in these times when the war drums are pounding in the distance, and everyone is in such dire straits, I really shouldn't have such leisurely whims. Even if I don't emulate the ancients who "slept on firewood and tasted gall," I should be a little more serious. In this era, "leisurely whims" are only for the likes of General XX, who, fulfilling an engagement with a foreign envoy, goes hunting in the countryside. How can I, a mere commoner, aspire to that?

However, last night I dreamed of West Lake again. But I was only standing on the embankment by the lake, staring intently, without moving my feet even half a step. What rippled in my eyes was neither the beauty of West Lake, nor the brilliance of spring, nor the lushness of the vegetation, nor the fragrance of the flowers, nor the swallows chatting and orioles warbling over the water, but rather the cuckoos crying blood and mountain torrents roaring. The groups of people writhing on the lake's surface and the hillside, I saw them clearly: they were corpses. And so I cried, not because my feet couldn't move, but because my mouth couldn't shout, only gurgling in my throat, unable to awaken those crowds of pleasure-seekers. Even if they don't know the hatred of a fallen nation, they should remotely listen, remotely listen to the sound of cannons from beyond the border, and see if it's escaping to the borderlands or rushing into the interior. I became anxious and panicked. Suddenly, a tall, thin shadow shot out in front of me. Someone was patting my shoulder: "You kid, why are you so foolish? Isn't this a world of singing and dancing now? Besides the cannons beyond the border shouting, shouting, what use is there anyway? You have to know that the sound of cannons from beyond the border can't penetrate the eardrums of the people, unless disaster comes to their own homes, see what happens, young man, let me take you to indulge and sink together, don't be foolish here!" "Thank you! My feet can't move, you go ahead!" After I replied, I still stared intently, staring at the corpse like a swarm of bees, suddenly, "Boom!" A heavy sound, as if it fell in the center of West Lake, the lake water splashing in all directions, and the people on the rampage all came to an end, I woke up suddenly, opened my eyes, the room had sparse sunlight jumping, I quickly put on my coat, got out of bed and started the busyness of life.

The Principal's Guard

— Bai Tao

A principal having a guard, the principal's guard actually detaining professors, privately imprisoning and brutally beating them, and all the faculty and students in the entire school are actually under the guns of the principal's guard, with no way to appeal for help. This is truly a shocking thing, and it can also be said to be a peculiar spectacle in the Chinese education world. If you don't believe it, please see the telegram from the entire faculty and students of National Sun Yat-sen University in Hong Kong on the 14th, supporting the tragic case of the forest farm:

The text of the telegram roughly says: Because a certain Zhang, the acting captain of the forest police team of the forest farm, privately dismissed five forest police officers, Hou, the professor and director of the forest farm, ordered the captain to reinstate the dismissed forest police officers because he had dismissed them without cause. As a result, Zou Libing, the nephew of Principal Zou and the captain of the forest police team, gathered more than ten members of the principal's guard and went straight to the forest farm, threatening Director Hou and forest farm staff members Huang and Lai with pistols aimed at their chests. Then, they detained Director Hou in the principal's office, falsely accusing Huang and Lai of being communists, brutally beating and seriously injuring them, and then locking them in the school police office with iron chains and large locks. Affairs Director Zou Jiu-cheng deliberately indulged evil and fostered traitors. Only after the faculty and students signed a petition and begged bitterly did they release the two men for medical treatment, and so on...

It was a chaotic and tumultuous situation. This ignorant person thought that the university had suddenly turned into a command headquarters or a detention center. Fortunately, the entire faculty and students signed a petition and begged bitterly, otherwise the lives of Professor Hou and Messrs. Huang and Lai would have been in great danger! However, Messrs. Huang and Lai had already been brutally beaten and seriously injured, and they had been chained with iron locks. Professor Hou was also imprisoned in the principal's office, and he had tasted the flavor of iron bars in the university!

Fortunately, this person's family is poor and cannot afford to go to university, otherwise I would be terrified of being imprisoned and becoming a prisoner in the school police office, where I would have to shout: "......

Seeking guarantees for more than 4,000 faculty and students, preserving the dignity of the sacred institution of learning, seeking the extension of human rights, ......" and enduring pain and sacrifice there, respectfully requesting national cultural organizations to uphold justice and provide sympathy and assistance! Not only would I be unable to study, but I would also have to anxiously call for help from the outside world for the sake of extending human rights. This is precisely where evil is being done!

If it really comes to a point where there is no way to appeal for help under the guns of the principal's guard, then one is not going to "study,"

but rather to "study death"! Alas!

Shop Assistant Communication

Spilled Water Can Be Recovered

Dear Editor:

I am a junior employee in a certain large store, 22 years old this year, and my monthly income is still abundant. I now have an extremely difficult problem to solve: when I was seventeen years old, my family arranged a marriage for me; at that time, I was still young, so I did not comment on this matter. The other party is also eighteen years old this year, so I originally intended to get married this winter. Last year, the other party was still studying at school and was seduced by a certain male classmate; at the end of last year, they agreed to elope and sent a letter requesting the other party's father to propose to my family to terminate the engagement; my father naturally agreed, and the engagement was terminated accordingly. Now, because the family of a certain male classmate does not allow the woman to return to her mother's home. After this, many people came to say, "Her previous conduct was excellent, and she was also intelligent, but she was temporarily bewitched by someone, and now she has completely repented,

I sincerely hope that my family can forgive her and reconnect the kinship of Qin and Jin." Her learning and character are indeed very good. She has completely repented, and I personally think that it is okay to re-establish the old agreement. However, people at home are absolutely opposed, saying how "reputation is at stake" and so on. If I really marry her, will it really affect my reputation? Please give me a reply. (omitted below)

Wang Yunlai respectfully submitted

X X X X

Editor's note: Whether Wang Jun's counterpart can really repent cannot be based entirely on the rumors of others; you must carefully investigate it yourself. If she really repents, then you can marry her without any harm. If her repentance is only out of necessity, then the results in the future will be terrible. As for the layer of reputation, because there are still many stubborn people in the current society, it is inevitable that it will be affected by them. However, this is a mistake in their concept, and you can ignore it!

Finally, we believe that a woman's social interaction can of course be open, but it is really necessary to avoid losing her body to others casually. Because after one mistake, even if you are ashamed and regretful, who can forgive you immediately?

His name should be Wang Guodong, Zhou Xichen replied.

"Ah! Wang Guodong"! Wu Yi's expression suddenly changed. He stood up straight and jumped off his seat,

His nearsighted eyes widened twice as large as usual. His arms were crossed in front of his chest, like a boxer standing upright. He remembered that three years ago, when he was still a puppet, Wang Yulin had written him a letter,

The general idea is: "The puppy Yulin, a student of Guo-dong, lost his mother in his early years, (Ms. Mao died in the second year Wu Yi came to Nanjing) lacking people to teach, his nature is special. He has been admitted to your school of business, and I beg you to take care of him at any time.

......" However, at that time, Wu Yi not only lost his power, but was also unable to take care of him, and he drank and drank all day long. He didn't take this matter to heart. Xiang thought that today, he would meet each other on a narrow road! How could he not panic and panic?

He also remembered that when Xiao Lin was four years old, he was already able to come and go alone. Because Jufen loved him so much, she always held him like a one- or two-year-old child. The hot weather made her sweat all over!

Also no complaint; once, she solemnly told Wu Yi: "You must sincerely love my Xiao Lin,

For example, if your son and Xiao Lin fall into the water at the same time, you must save Xiao Lin first, and then save your son. This is my good friend"! At that time, Wu Yi also gave her a satisfactory reply, he said: "I will love him as you do"!

Now that Jufen is dead, these few words are still echoing in his ears, but in such a situation, how can he偏護 his "lover's son".

Movie Special

Where Are Our Works with a Strong Sense of Consciousness?

— Qian Taisheng

It is undeniable that the year 1933 may be the year when our decadent and confused film industry turns around and awakens. Looking at the recent works of various companies, from "A Woman's Cry" recently released to "Vitality" about to be released, and the previously released works such as "Three Modern Women", "City Night", "Morning in the Metropolis", "Raging Torrent" and so on, we can find that they are standing on the same

The front is to make more life-affirming works.

There is no doubt that they want to seize this dynamic and active era and give a painful attack on the so-called capitalist society, and want to use the same subject matter to clarify the significance of the new life of workers and peasants! However, by making a rigorous analysis of all the works,

We cannot but admit that they have only a partial success.

In "A Woman's Cry", the director obviously did not grasp the main part of the whole play, so the whole play is inevitably shrouded in a hazy veil, and the most tense completion of the whole play is missed in the loose part of the whole play. It is said that there are also many scenes introducing the life of female workers in "Vitality", and we don't want to say anything before it is released.

In "Three Modern Women", it tells us that the most "modern" women are the women who are advancing and revolutionizing, and what is introduced on the screen is a painting of a worker's wharf, saying that this is the suffering of workers' lives! In the ending scene, the consciousness is especially unhealthy. It writes that this young young master can give up his life of arbitrary enjoyment and leave the city with his beloved female worker. Although it wants to show the awakening of the young master, it actually only writes that the young master is infatuated and crazy for this beautiful female worker. The reason why he left his usual life of bourgeois pleasure is not revolution, not light, but only fascination for a woman.

What do "City Night" and "Morning in the Metropolis" tell us? One ending slogan is: "Everyone go back to the countryside!" One result is to write "Go to the light!" But where is the countryside? What is "our" place of light? What is the place where the general working class of farmers and workers is not squeezed and exploited? Is "Peach Blossom Garden" and "Paradise" the same fantasy as this "countryside" or "place of light"?

What "Raging Torrent" writes is an exposure of the crime of rural composition, and the formation of a great flood. It writes about the violent and dangerous gentlemen in the countryside, and it writes about who is the culprit of the great flood. But whether the culprit it writes is the real culprit, or only a sinner created by the environment, and cannot bear the name of the culprit

The above-mentioned works, their reference to new themes, cannot but make us feel sympathetic, but in the result of the performance, the positive introduction of depicting workers and rural areas has been neglected, and it has become a work with vague consciousness, which is indeed the most regrettable fact in our emerging film industry in 1933.

However, as far as the production company is concerned, according to what we know, "Three Modern Women" once had a scene of a large-scale strike by telephone female workers; the "Raging Torrent" was originally a scene of peasant riots, which were all deleted. The company is afraid of touching the authorities' taboo, so they have to go in a gentle direction; but because they use new themes and consciousness, they have to make newer works, and the result is this contradictory performance that makes people feel neither painful nor itchy.

In this squeezed environment, in this sour and bitter era, when can we see a work with a strong sense of consciousness?

Feelings After Watching "The Spring Colors of the Luoyang Palace"

"You are Princess妲拉喀挪華"

After watching "A Woman's Cry"

— Li Qiong

Regarding "A Woman's Cry", it is obviously based on the theme of women's liberation. So our women are really worthy of concern. When I walked out of the Central Theater after watching this film, I felt that the screenwriter was very clear about the current situation of our petty bourgeoisie women in China. But we are not satisfied with this; why? Because in fact, Chinese women are already "shouting" loudly, and it is by no means the time to "shout" as the film says. What's more, this film has not yet "shouted" out. In other words: it is that the producer's instructions for the way out are so empty and ambiguous. A revolutionary woman, Shaoying, should be a major figure in the play, but the director only said a few words about her in the subtitles, which is of course very insufficient. When the heroine Ye Lian has gone through several stimuli and is determined to strive and fight against the evil forces, then she must be a strong and brave typical woman who resists, but what is shown in the play is a shameful and very timid girl, at most it is just unwilling to be downgraded in personality. At the same time, is this idealistic concept of chastity more important than other more important issues? Secondly, at the end of the film, the director very seriously took a picture of the statue of peace on the Bund, which is really incomprehensible, is it saying that as long as Ye Lian is aware, it will be world peace immediately? If so, it will make us suspect that the director is too nervous.

However, as a whole, this "A Woman's Cry" is after all a new work that grasps the times, so we still have great hopes for the producers of this film.

"A Woman's Cry" – Where Does the Cry Come From?

— Xi Zong

The awareness expressed in "A Woman's Cry" cannot be said to be distorted; however, in terms of performance technique and structure, it is a failure! One reason is that the screenwriter lacks real-life experience, but also, experience is indeed a major factor. This kind of "woman's cry," even if the throat is hoarse from shouting, will never awaken the two hundred million sleeping female compatriots! Truly, rather than calling it "A Woman's Cry," it would be more appropriate to call it "The Oppression of Women."

The scenes unfolded on the screen do not show any kind of "cry," nor do they indicate a bright future. The female protagonist, Ye Lian, enters society and encounters only suffering and oppression. This can hardly be called a "cry"; the "cry" simply does not exist.

There are also some contradictions and errors here: for example, when Wang Dama steals a bracelet from Ye Lian's house after the robbery, the bracelet would never be placed in a drawer of an empty cabinet, because the robbers would have ransacked the place and would not have left the bracelet behind. These are some contradictions; after Ye Lian's younger sister is deceived and locked in a room, her hair is sometimes permed and sometimes childlike – these are some errors.

Ministry of Education Plans to Establish a Film Bureau

— Zhao Kuangyin

The Ministry of Education recently accepted the suggestions of Chu Minyi and Chen Guofu to establish a Film Bureau, hoping to thoroughly improve China's film industry. After repeated discussions, the Ministry decided to merge and reorganize the existing film censorship committees of the two departments within the Ministry to establish a National Film Bureau. The drafting of the regulations has been handed over to the Secretariat. Its future work will be divided into: (1) compiling film scripts that promote national spirit and depict the hardships of the people, for adoption by film companies nationwide; (2) producing films that promote national spirit and depict the lives of the people, for rental and purchase by theaters nationwide;

(3) producing films about various national undertakings, for broadcasting in various countries.

Generally speaking, "A Woman's Cry" is not as good as "Torrent" and "Flower of Freedom."

The Film Novel "Tarakonova" (7)

— Meihua

After sending Tarakonova to the monastery, Orlov's soul continued to follow her. He always felt uneasy about sending her to the monastery. He secretly went to the monastery several times to see Tarakonova, but this girl, scarred in both mind and body, could no longer see him! He was repeatedly rejected. He sighed deeply at this solemn monastery, lowered his head, and walked slowly, imagining Princess Tarakonova lying inside, wondering if she was still sighing or resentful.

In fact, Tarakonova would not resent him; not only would she not resent him, but she loved him wholeheartedly! When she lay alone in bed, listening to the church bells, she would think of the palace on the coast of Italy! She would think of the cheering scenes when Orlov invited her onto the warship. Yes, everything still appeared before her eyes, but where was Orlov?

"Oh, my love, will you ever come?" she moaned weakly; sometimes hearing the chirping of birds in the courtyard, she suspected it was Orlov's voice; sometimes, when the door creaked, she imagined it was Orlov's footsteps. Her eye sockets had sunken deeply, her cheekbones were frighteningly high, she yearned, she opened her eyes wide in hope, and that last spark of desire still burned like a flame!

Orlov finally came! Everyone knew that this might be their last meeting. Not allowing them to meet would leave them with lifelong grief that they could not bear even in death; but allowing them to meet was against the rules. Finally, a screen was set up in front of her bed! Orlov lowered his head, walking into the prison cell like a criminal. His heart ached, he was filled with remorse, he wanted to rush forward and embrace her, crying bitterly! But he thought of having already committed one sin, and he shouldn't add to his crimes. He could only lower his head and shout, "Tarakonova, please forgive me!" Hearing this voice, which was so familiar, she knew it was Orlov; "Oh, my love, I still love you!" But she could no longer speak, her lips quivered, and a faint smile appeared on her pale face. She knew in her heart that Orlov had come to her bedside, but poor Orlov, he did not have the chance to see her last smile.

As Orlov walked slowly out of the monastery, the sound of a mournful song was carried on the wind. He cocked his ear and listened, looking inside with both eyes. A dark figure lay on a stretcher, and four nuns were weeping, heading straight for the mortuary, with Princess Possetti wiping away tears with a handkerchief, weeping behind.

Orlov's dark shadow also disappeared with this mournful sound. (The End)

Key Points of the Latest Library Architecture (2)

Songfu

The Position of the Reader

The position of the reader includes three aspects: 1. Reading Room;

2. Card Catalog; 3. Circulation Desk. The most important of these is the last one. Because it is the intermediary between the books in the library and the reader, it is the center of the library. Because the three elements of the library are books,

readers, and librarians – all meet here. In theory, the circulation desk is located in the middle of the book stacks and the reading room. In practice, many are located in this position. The position occupied by the circulation desk should be able to take care of the largest position in front or on both sides, such as the entrance, corridor,

catalog, card catalog, and reading room. At the same time, it should be close to the book stacks for easy retrieval or return of books. There should be ample space in front of and behind the circulation desk. The most important thing is that the circulation desk has sufficient light. It is best to have light from two sides. Because using skylights, it is extremely dark in the early morning.

As for working during the daytime, it is especially inappropriate to use electric lights.

There are also many different kinds of reading rooms, such as general reading rooms, children's reading rooms, reference rooms, magazine rooms, special reading rooms, study rooms, discussion rooms, etc. The various uses are different, and the size, location, and structure are also different. Therefore, it is difficult to generalize. However, in ordinary circumstances, the simpler and more direct the reading room, the better. Avoid circuitous routes. Although theorists often consider circular or octagonal reading rooms unsatisfactory, they are not a major problem if arranged properly. If the architecture is well done, it is also very elegant. For example, Oxford's Radcliffe Library,

London's British Museum, Washington's Congressional Library, and New York's Columbia University Library are all very magnificent.

In the reading room, the most important issue is lighting. If the light comes from one side, then the width of the room cannot exceed 50 to 60% of the height of the window. If the room is 14 or 15 feet high, the window sill can be 4 1/2 or even 5 feet above the ground. Therefore, the surrounding walls have 3 1/2 to 4 1/2 feet of space to place bookshelves, connecting continuously. The higher the window sill, the farther the light reaches. A reading room with about two sides of light should be more than thirty feet wide and fifteen feet high to be suitable. Skylight illumination is not unusable, but it is definitely too dark in the early morning. Reading rooms cannot rely solely on skylight illumination.

Reading rooms, except in special circumstances – such as being limited to reviewing books within the room and not being able to take books from the book stacks – should be close to the book stacks and near the circulation desk, so that the person in charge of the circulation desk can also take care of the readers in the reading room.

The Position of the Librarian

The position of the librarian is divided into: 1. Library room and general affairs room, etc.; 2. Cataloging room, card making room, etc.; 3. Registration room, branch library room, etc.; 4. Binding room, printing room, etc.; 5.

Storage room, dining room, retirement room, etc.; 6. Miscellaneous service room, etc. In large libraries, there are also committee rooms, board rooms, etc. It is difficult to set ordinary rules for the layout of each room. However, the most important thing is that the location of each room should be suitable for the tasks being performed. Entry and exit should be convenient, and the lighting should be sufficient. Special attention should be paid to the economy of operations, the convenience of interconnection, and the comfort of the environment.

Research on Road Construction

Yun

The title of road construction has already become the key plan for China today. And it is the common effort of the whole country. This is a sign of China's future. However, there are countless ways to manage roads. It cannot be fully explained in one or two words. Now, generally speaking, the elements can be divided into two points. The first is the width of the road. The second is the type of construction. The width of the road surface cannot be fixed. Economic distance and the amount of traffic must be carefully calculated in advance. The so-called width of the highway includes two vehicles (the size must be the same) and refers to the breadth that allows them to travel freely at the same time. This is enough to allow two vehicles to pass safely. When turning, it is not necessary to yield to each other.

The construction of highways is also based on the above principles to determine the type. Local land, local materials, freight costs for materials purchased from other places,

and wages, etc., should all be discussed one by one without negligence.

There are about two types of road construction, called "solid" and "semi-solid" respectively. Solid roads are mostly paved with "three-in-one soil." The cost is very high. Speaking from China's current situation and what is needed by society, semi-solid roads are more suitable. However, the construction method must be distinguished according to the trends of each locality.

The foundation of the road is very important. The distinction between good and bad depends on the materials used and the amount of expense.

The method of establishing the foundation is to use large stones sandwiched with gravel as the bottom layer. And sand is laid on the surface of the road.

However, if this material is lacking, other things can be used instead. As for the size of the object, it depends on the quality of the road and the condition of the land. But in the long run, problems will inevitably arise.

Impermeability to rainwater is also an important point for roads. The method of achieving this depends on the condition of the road surface. The usual procedure is to use asphalt or a mixture containing asphalt and other paving materials mixed and rolled onto the road surface to make it hard and flat.

The method of draining rainwater is also important. And it must be studied. Because the speed of drainage is closely related to the safety and lifespan of the road. The best way is to dig adequate ditches on both sides of the road.

The center of the road should be built with a sufficient arch. This depends on the characteristics of the road surface material. The width of the road determines the height of the arch.

Generally, before a highway is built, it is best to allow traffic to pass first. After a year or six months, pave the final layer of the road surface to allow it to be filled and prepared. The road base can then be stabilized. Maintaining the road surface is also important. If repairs are made at any time according to the traffic situation, the weather, and the condition of the road surface, the cost will not be high, and the road will always be in perfect condition, instead of appearing in a rugged and skewed state.

The load-bearing capacity of the road surface must be limited. Vehicles without automobile tires should not be allowed to pass. As for the maintenance methods, such as oiling and repairing, there is no need to cut off traffic. It can be organized on one side, leaving the other side for vehicles to pass. This is more convenient.

Further Discussion on Urban Design

Gu Jieyun

For the past ten years, we Chinese have been talking about new municipal administration, but when we examine what is called municipal administration in China, it is far from the municipal administration of Europe and America, and even further from the so-called ideal municipal administration. There are many reasons for this, roughly speaking, there are the following: first, due to the difficulty of local finances; second, because most of the cities in China are already built, so what is called municipal administration is only to improve existing cities, rather than starting new regulations. From the experience of municipal administration, we can observe that improving cities is always more difficult than creating new cities, so the progress of municipal administration is naturally slow; third, due to the lack of consolidated urban design, whenever a city should be improved or a new city should be created in advance,

there should be a consolidated design, such as the determination of routes, traffic design such as water conservancy, electric lights, drainage ditches, hygiene and public and private buildings, etc., all must have far-sighted and comprehensive calculations in advance, otherwise only taking care of the current piecemeal improvements, then when the population and material resources increase rapidly in ten or twenty years, the original various things will either not be applicable or will not be able to meet the needs of the environment, causing the entire city's municipal administration to fall into a stagnant state. In addition, incidental drawbacks occur, such as the sharp increase in land prices due to the development of municipal administration, speculation rises, causing the poor to suffer even more, and the separation of industrial and commercial and residential areas, with dust and coal gas fumes, hindering public health and so on, all of which are fatal wounds to the entire city. This is due to the lack of an overall plan at the time.

When we talk about municipal administration, we often take Shanghai as a model. Although the buildings in the public and French concessions are roughly scaled, its shortcomings are really too numerous to mention. Let's start with the buildings to prove it. The buildings in the Shanghai concessions are seen by ordinary people as magnificent and beautiful, but those who know better think they are of uneven height and not very beautiful. As for the issue of demarcation, we dare not blindly follow. Looking at the trade area of ​​the Great Roads of England and France in Shanghai, there are residences and factories built at will, without any order, which hinders public health and public safety is really not small. Further, let's talk about trams. Generally, streets that can build tramways must be wide, such as the Fifth Road of the Public Concession and the East New Bridge of the French Concession, where the streets are so narrow that trams actually run through them, so there are often many obstacles in traffic. Moreover, according to the new municipal system of Europe and America,

air lawns should be built in trade areas,

for merchants to rest at will. The Shanghai Public Concession only has a very small number of lawns along the municipal port and the Suzhou River. It is very inconvenient for us. There are many other shortcomings, which I will not elaborate on now. However, from this place, we can see that the municipal administration of the Shanghai concessions is not very good. As for the municipal administration organized by the Chinese, it is even worse than the municipal administration of the concessions. Since Shanghai's municipal weaknesses are so numerous, summarizing them, it is nothing more than that there was no overall urban design for the entire city at the time. After the city developed, it became difficult to change, which caused the city to fall into an incomplete state. Therefore, those who talk about municipal administration in the future should pay attention to the issue of urban planning. Before a city is to be managed, it should have an overall design with a far-sighted vision, and then implement it step by step, so that it can avoid repeating the mistakes of its predecessors. But what is called urban design? Now I will briefly explain it as follows:

Urban design is the science of planning and building cities. Its purpose is to create an urban environment that is convenient for transportation, hygienic for housing, and beautiful in environment. Therefore, from the broad sense of municipal administration, almost every part of the municipal administrative organization has a close relationship with it. Because urban design originally includes the design of docks, wharves, railways, commercial operations, streets, subways, roadways, the planning of internal and external urban transportation, and other things such as water materials, canals, electric lights, public housing, parks, playgrounds, private buildings, public health, etc., all of which belong to the time when urban design is being done, and should be carefully planned, in order to seek the beauty of urban construction, the development of industry and commerce, and the residents' peaceful and prosperous lives, etc., must have a good design.

Moreover, Avinoir, a well-known American urban design research expert, once described the general outline of urban design in his writings, saying that the first purpose of urban design is to protect the health of the citizens and address the housing problem, the water problem, the drainage problem, the public market problem,

and many other hygiene problems, etc., all included. The second purpose is to operate citizens' highly effective labor, such as the issue of transportation agencies, the appropriate configuration and arrangement of commercial districts, industrial districts, and residential areas, all included. The third purpose is to enable citizens to use their leisure time to seek healthy development of body and mind, such as parks, playgrounds, and many other issues, from which we can clearly understand the meaning of urban design.

Ordinary people often think that urban design belongs to engineering problems. It must be known that in the design of a city, engineering problems are only a part, and other things such as hygiene design, financial design, and legal regulations are as important as engineering. From this, it can be known that when a city is designed, not only should engineering personnel be collected, but also medical, legal, and economic talents should be recruited to seek simultaneous development in all aspects.

Research on Doors and Windows

Shuang

Although doors and windows are subsidiary parts of houses, they are also very important for people's daily life, because doors and windows can provide natural light and air circulation. Therefore, when we build houses, we should pay special attention to door and window equipment: especially public buildings,

such as hotels, theaters, companies, etc., should have more doors and windows to facilitate access and sufficient light, because this is indirectly related to public health and convenience.

Like the houses in our country in the past, when you stepped inside, you felt dark and damp. The biggest reason was the lack of windows and insufficient light; this affected people's daily life, so this kind of architecture is no longer applicable and has been eliminated in modern times.

Now let's talk about "doors" first.

Western architecture, such as residences, companies, and schools, all use panel doors. Other less important places use frame doors. As for factory buildings, which are originally intended to be sturdy, steel doors are used the most.

Let's talk about "windows" again:

The position of the window directly affects the light, so we must pay attention to the method of its layout. The area occupied by the windows of ordinary school buildings must not be less than 20 to 25 percent of the floor area. There are several things to pay attention to regarding light: (1) The source of light must be continuous; (2) The light must be sufficient and distributed throughout the room; (3) The position of the window should avoid direct sunlight and make it reflected light.

(Window area) The size of the area where light enters must be determined by the depth of the room, the height, and the position of the window. The area of windows in school buildings has already been mentioned above. In factory buildings, according to the current trend, it is best to make both roof skylights and wall windows out of glass; but the area of ordinary windows must be 50 to 60 percent of the floor area.

(Window height) If the windows in the room are only on one side of the wall, in order to make the light sufficient throughout the room, the depth of the room must not exceed three times the height of the window. If there are windows on both sides of the wall, then their height cannot be less than a quarter of the depth of the house.

(Types of windows) There are roughly three types of windows: (1) fixed window frames, (2) movable window frames, (3) pivot window frames.

Movable window frames are also divided into single-sash movable and double-sash movable. The structure is a kind of window frame with pulleys installed inside, one end balanced with weight. Due to the pulling force, the pulley rotates, and the window can move up and down.

The movement of the entire pivot window frame depends on the pivot on one side of the window for rotation, so many buildings use this type.

(Steel windows) The architecture of the new era of the 20th century. No matter what material is used, it is manufactured using scientific methods. Steel windows are one of them. Generally, slightly taller buildings use steel windows instead of wooden windows. Its advantages are: the material is solid, and it is not easily damaged even after being eroded by wind and rain.

And it can also increase the appearance of the building. If a building in a busy area of the city is equipped with steel windows,

the vibrations of vehicles can be avoided.

Therefore, I dare say that steel windows can gain an invincible position in architecture.
